# Operation Log

Chronological record of significant operations. Each entry is its own file under `log/`; this page is the reverse-chronological index. See [concepts/parallel-session-coordination.md](concepts/parallel-session-coordination.md) for why.

- [2026-05-31 -- Act tier-shell: objective<->observation link + per-objective feed + Observe provenance chip](log/2026-05-31-act-tier-shell-objective-observation-link.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (three explicit-path slice commits `389bff36` Slice A schema+store -> `67926c85` Slice B Act feed -> `66aee783` Slice C Observe chip; not pushed). Closed the two follow-ups the record-observation ADR deferred *because* `ObserveDataPoint` carried no link back to its objective; operator explicitly requested the schema change that ADR had listed as rejected. **Slice A:** schema gains `sourceObjectiveId: z.string().nullable().default(null)` after `sourceFeedEntryId` (operator-chosen name, parity with `sourceActionId`/`sourceFeedEntryId`); `.default(null)` makes the output type require it so `tsc` enumerated every literal (seed factory, `routeToDataPoint` feed projection, 3 test fixtures -> `null`); `observeDataPointStore` gains `getByObjective`/`getActiveByObjective` selectors + persist `version` 1->2 with a backfill migrate; NEW conformance test `observeDataPointObjectiveLink.test.ts` (3: default-null backward-compat, field round-trip, every `UNIVERSAL_PLAN_OBJECTIVES` id resolves a title via `findObjectiveAcrossCatalogues`). **Slice B:** `handleRecord` stamps `sourceObjectiveId: objective.id`; "This need's activity" becomes a real per-objective feed (`useObserveDataPointStore((s)=>s.byProject)` + `useMemo`-filter by `sourceObjectiveId`, newest-first via `Date.parse(capturedAt)`; rows = `formatActyTimestamp` + capturedBy + `readNote(measurementValue)`; new `.actyList`/`.actyRow`/`.actyMeta`/`.actyNote` CSS in the `.evCard` vocabulary); **repeat recordings allowed** (operator choice -- removed the session-local `recorded` lock + its `useEffect`, button stays `disabled={!ready}`, the feed row is the confirmation); import trimmed to `useMemo`. No supersession hazard: Act points are `locationGeometry:null`, so `computeSupersession` never pairs them. **Slice C:** Observe `DomainObservationList` renders a gold objective-title provenance chip via `findObjectiveAcrossCatalogues(point.sourceObjectiveId)?.title` in `.rowHead` (after `virtualTag`); domain-only/field-log rows (null) unaffected, no raw id leak; new `.objectiveTag` pill distinct from the dashed `.virtualTag`. **Verified:** apps/web + packages/shared tsc clean for my files (foreign TanStack `routeTree.gen.ts` regeneration churn -- compass/true-north routes in ActTools/ActCommandCentrePage/ObserveCommandCentrePage/V3LifecycleSidebar/etc. -- isolated via `git status --porcelain`, every erroring file foreign-modified, none mine; re-ran once the tree settled -> WEB_EXIT=0); live preview ("Baseline Test Homestead", `/v3/.../act`, no WebGL hang) -- recorded 2 observations on `s2-terrain` -> 2 feed rows newest-first + button stayed armed + `localStorage['ogden-observe-data-points']` both points carried `sourceObjectiveId:"s2-terrain"`; Observe Climate Domain Detail showed 2 gold "Survey terrain & topography" chips on those rows + NONE on the legacy null row; screenshot captured; 2 test points cleaned up. **Supersedes decision #2** of [[decisions/2026-05-31-atlas-act-record-observation-emits-datapoint]] in part (domain-only link -> domain link PLUS objective provenance). - [2026-05-31 -- Act tier-shell: s1-vision form save marks matching checklist item complete](log/2026-05-31-act-tier-shell-s1vision-form-checklist.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (explicit-path commit `2624c3ca`, 2 files: `planStratumStore.ts`, `ActTierShell.tsx`; 3 ahead of origin, not pushed). Closed the gap where saving a Vision tile modal (s1-vision form tools) persisted the text but left the corresponding right-rail checklist item unchecked. **`planStratumStore.ts`**: added `setItemComplete(projectId, objectiveId, itemId)` to the `PlanStratumProgressState` interface + implementation. Idempotent add-only action (`if (current.includes(itemId)) return s` guard) -- safe to call from form-save handlers where `toggleItem` would risk accidentally unchecking a manually-ticked item on a re-save. No new state fields; no persist version bump. **`ActTierShell.tsx`**: `handleFormSave` updated to call `usePlanStratumProgressStore.getState().setItemComplete(id, objectiveId, formId)` after `saveVisionForm`; guard on `objectiveId` being non-null; dependency array extended from `[id]` to `[id, objectiveId]`. The `formId` IS the checklist item id by catalog design (1:1 mapping per `actToolCatalog`). `usePlanStratumProgressStore` was already imported. **Verified:** save "Primary purpose" -> `s1-vision-c1` ticked; save "Success criteria" -> `['s1-vision-c1','s1-vision-c2']` / 2 boxes checked; re-save "Primary purpose" -> still 2 (idempotent); hard reload -> both ids survive rehydration. Full `apps/web` tsc 0 errors (3 independent runs). CSRA model untouched ([[fiqh-csra-erased-2026-05-04]]); ASCII-only copy. - [2026-05-31 -- Act tier-shell: Evidence capture + s1-vision forms wired to persisted store](log/2026-05-31-act-tier-shell-evidence-store-persistence.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (explicit-path commit `e6f06475`, 3 files: `actEvidenceStore.ts` NEW, `ActTierExecutionPanel.tsx`, `ActTierShell.tsx`; not pushed). Closed the "visual-first, not persisted" gap noted in the execution-panel header comment after the three slice commits. New `actEvidenceStore` (`ogden-act-evidence`, v1): `byProject[projectId][objectiveId]: EvidenceCapture` (photo counts, confirms, note text + notesSaved keyed by `descriptorId`); `visionForms[projectId][formId]: string`. Actions: `addPhoto` (capped at `maxTarget`, no-op at cap), `setConfirm`/`saveNote` (idempotent), `updateNote` (atomically clears saved flag), `saveVisionForm`. `EMPTY_CAPTURE` frozen constant prevents the Zustand v5 `getSnapshot` infinite re-render loop. Checklist completion writes to the SHARED `planStratumStore.toggleItem` (not actEvidenceStore) so Act and Plan use one source of truth for progress. `ActTierExecutionPanel` replaced 5 `useState` hooks with selectors against the two stores; each action selected individually to avoid composite-selector object churn. `ActTierShell` replaced `formValues` useState with `visionForms` selector (with `EMPTY_FORMS` frozen fallback -- the same getSnapshot fix); `handleFormSave` calls `useActEvidenceStore.getState().saveVisionForm(...)` (imperative, not render-phase). **Verified:** write -> objective-switch -> hard reload -- all three stores confirmed via `import('/src/store/actEvidenceStore.ts')` + DOM probes; `completedIds: ['s2-terrain-c1']`, `photoCount: 1`, `noteText: 'Test note for s2-terrain'`, `noteSaved: true` survived reload; UI re-hydrated from store on page load (checkbox checked, textarea populated, count badge `1/3`). New shared module `relationships/objectiveEvidence.ts` (no app deps, so catalogue + relevance map + resolver all live in `@ogden/shared`): `EvidenceKind = photo|confirm|note`; `EVIDENCE_CATALOG` (5; original 3 verbatim + `site-photo`/`measurement-confirm`); `OBJECTIVE_EVIDENCE_OVERRIDE` keyed by the REAL 19 universal objective ids (`summary-note` on all 19, **`route-passable` ONLY on `s5-access`+`s2-infrastructure`** -- the fix, `measurement-confirm` on the measured/spec objectives); `STRATUM_EVIDENCE_DEFAULT` backstop; `getObjectiveEvidence` resolves `OVERRIDE[id] ?? STRATUM_DEFAULT[stratumId] ?? ['summary-note']` -> descriptors, exported from the ROOT barrel. `ActTierExecutionPanel.tsx` swaps the three scalar evidence vars for descriptor-keyed records + a `renderEvidenceCard` helper (markup byte-identical) + `{evidence.map(...)}`; evidence state stays LOCAL/ephemeral. New conformance test `objectiveEvidenceCoverage.test.ts` (6 invariants, the guard whose absence let the tool override map rot) -- **6/6**. **Slice 3** (CSS + small JSX): the tools rail framed one category at a time behind a native vertical scrollbar; operator wanted vertically-stacked circles/dashes that indicate AND navigate. `ActTierCategorizedToolsRail.tsx` builds an indexable `visibleCats` list, tracks the framed category via an `IntersectionObserver` (root = the row, highest-ratio sets `activeIndex`), and renders a `.toolsDots` `<nav>` (one `.toolDot` per category, **only when >1**) inside a new `.toolsBody` flex row; each dot `scrollIntoView`s its `.toolCat`. CSS hides the native scrollbar (`scrollbar-width:none` + `::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}`) and styles `.toolDot` (7px circle -> 16px gold dash when active). **Verified:** apps/web + packages/shared tsc exit 0; conformance 6/6; live preview ("Baseline Test Homestead", `/v3/.../act`) -- s1-vision -> Summary note only, s2-terrain -> Checkpoint photos + Summary note (no route-passable), s5-access -> all three; s2-ecology -> 2 dots, scrollbar hidden, dot-2 click scrolled the row + moved the active dash, s2-terrain -> 0 dots; two screenshots. - [2026-05-29 -- Plan Tier detail-panel: hide MAP ACTIVATION section when no overlays bound](log/2026-05-29-plan-tier-detail-panel-hide-empty-map.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (1 file: `apps/web/src/v3/plan/tiers/ObjectiveDetailPanel.tsx`). JSX-only follow-up to [[decisions/2026-05-27-atlas-plan-tier-shell-phase1]] Slice 1.6. Steward flagged a screenshot of the ObjectiveDetailPanel showing the "MAP ACTIVATION" strip empty-state ("No overlays bound to this objective.") with a 260px satellite map still rendering underneath -- *"why is the map view here? It should not be."* Root cause: `MapActivationStrip` + `<div className={css.mapBody}><ObjectiveMap/></div>` rendered **unconditionally**, while only the strip's message gated on `objective.defaultOverlayBundle.length === 0` (inside OLOS `OverlayBundleStrip`); all 8 seeded objectives have `defaultOverlayBundle: []`, so an empty strip + a pointless map showed on every objective. Fix: derive `const hasOverlays = objective.defaultOverlayBundle.length > 0` and wrap the strip + map in `{hasOverlays && (<>...</>)}` -- the exact inverse of the empty-state condition, so the **whole** MAP ACTIVATION region (eyebrow + message + map) unmounts when no overlays are bound (steward-confirmed scope via AskUserQuestion) and reappears once a bundle is non-empty. Gated on `defaultOverlayBundle` not `activeOverlayIds` (stays visible while toggling individual overlays). Out of scope: `MapActivationStrip`/`OverlayBundleStrip` untouched (shared with `ObjectiveWorkspace`, [[feedback-no-deletion]]); no seed change; no CSS change (`.panel` has no `gap`, so removal leaves none). **Verified:** `tsc --noEmit` exit 0 / empty output (clean, no new errors); live `preview_eval` on project `d2708c91` across both panel states -- `t0-vision` (COMPLETE + review banner) and `t1-land-baseline` (READY, no banner) both show `_mapBody`, map canvas, "Map activation" eyebrow, and "No overlays bound" message all absent, panel flowing header -> (banner) -> YOUR DECISIONS with no gap; **screenshot captured** this session (tab visible, `document.hidden === false` -- unlike the sibling column-width task). Reappearance case sound by construction (bundled const not runtime-mutable; guard is the boolean inverse of the proven empty-state). No ADR (visibility tweak too narrow; precedent the sibling entry + `1bc907d4` / `a6ee7ae8`). Explicit-path commit (3 files, mirrors `63459f5f`); foreign WIP from parallel sessions left out per [[feedback-no-deletion]]; divergence-checked before push per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]. CSRA model untouched; ASCII-only copy.

- [2026-05-29 -- projectType normalization: stop project:create 422ing on sync](log/2026-05-29-projecttype-normalization-422-fix.md) -- **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (commit `fe367966`, 3 files: `store/projectStore.ts`, `lib/syncQueue.ts`, `lib/syncService.ts`). Continuation of the [[2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]] thread: that fix bounded the sync queue so a permanently-failing op could no longer OOM the renderer, but left the *cause* of the validation failures unfixed and unnamed (the client discarded the server's `details[]`). This session root-caused it -- OLOS carries two project-type vocabularies, kebab-case **archetype** (`regenerative-farm`, `v3/true-north/trueNorthConfig.ts`) and the snake_case server **`projectType`** (`regenerative_farm`, the Zod `ProjectType` enum); `createProject` persisted the raw value, so a kebab archetype could leak in and `project:create` 422'd on sync, the circuit breaker then dropping the op (unsyncable on-device). Live diagnosis named the offender as **"Phase 4 Smoke"** (`regenerative-farm`) -- correcting the 2026-05-25 ADR's provisional "Moontrance Creek" / "Test Vision Project" attribution (Moontrance Creek is `projectType: null` / valid; "Test Vision Project" was a transient vision-builder fixture, [[2026-05-25-atlas-stage-zero-vision-builder]]); a dated `> [!warning] Correction` callout was added there. **Three-tier fix:** persist `migrate` v4 -> v5 repairs existing records via `normalizeProjectType` (kebab archetype -> enum via `ARCHETYPE_TO_PROJECT_TYPE`, valid pass-through, unknown -> syncable null); `createProject` normalizes on write (prevent recurrence); `describeSyncError` folds the server `details: [{ path, message }]` into `op.lastError` + the create-failure log (so the next 422 names the field). **Verified:** web `tsc --noEmit` clean; live `ogden-projects` migrated to version 5 with 0 schema offenders across 40 projects (typeCounts `{ "(null)": 4, homestead: 9, multi_enterprise: 16, regenerative_farm: 11 }`), clean projects untouched; `git diff --cached --name-only` confirmed only the 3 source files staged. **Carry-over (corrected 2026-05-29):** the [[2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]] handler-swallow deferral was already closed the same day by [[decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-sync-circuit-breaker]] (`84bb8e91`) -- `executeQueuedOp` rethrows so `flush()` counts retries and drops exhausted ops via `handleExhaustedOp`; `describeSyncError` (this slice) makes such a drop name the offending field. Genuinely-open deferral: the human-gated two-device E2E + `FEATURE_SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` rollout. Not pushed (out-of-band rebase rule). ADR [[decisions/2026-05-29-atlas-projecttype-normalization-422-fix]]; corrects [[decisions/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]]; CSRA model untouched; ASCII-only copy.

- [2026-05-28 ÔÇö Scoped Views Epic design pass (Phase 5 Slice 5.5 re-scope)](log/2026-05-28-scoped-views-epic-design.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. **Design-only ÔÇö no implementation code.** Re-scoped the one-line "Slice 5.5 ÔÇö Contractor/Landowner scoped views (frontend-only, hook signature unchanged)" carry-over from [[log/2026-05-28-per-project-home-slice54]] into a **four-slice epic** after reading the ratified `OLOS_Project_Home_Spec_v1` (sections 1.3/4/5/6/7/8) against the code. The literal carry-over collapsed on three walls ÔÇö (1) `memberStore.myRole` is a single slot (no per-project role map to filter a portfolio on), (2) `useProjectRole` only fetches when logged in + Portfolio Home reads the localStorage store, so a naive role filter empties the portfolio in the dominant offline/demo mode, (3) frontend filtering is not the spec's data-layer 403 (7.2/8.5) ÔÇö and the spec is itself an epic (section 5 contractor task-only view, section 6 landowner read-only shareable progress view, section 7 contractor access expiry). Two verifications de-risked it: the API already gates ~every route on `authenticate -> resolveProjectRole -> requireRole(...)` (~22 callsites per `rbac.ts`), and the landowner view has a real foundation in the existing `v3/observe/dashboard/presentation/` suite + `presentationShareStore` + `ObserveShareViewerPage` + the `portal/` public-link API. Sharpest enforcement finding: `contractor` currently aliases to `designer` (`projectRoleCapabilities.ts:158`) with `{read, comment, edit}` over the whole project, so a contractor session satisfies every `requireRole('owner', 'designer')` gate today ÔÇö full Plan/Observe access (Slice 5.1 flagged this as a deliberate placeholder pending "future Phase 5 slices"; 5.5a/5.5c own breaking it). **Three decisions locked via AskUserQuestion:** (1) re-scope as epic + design first (vs. ship a narrow frontend slice / build substrate then filter); (2) foundational principle ÔÇö scoped views are an **authenticated + synced** capability, local-only/offline always renders full single-owner view (rejected: mandatory backend-backing; mirroring roles into the local store); (3) view order **Team -> Contractor -> Landowner** (steady risk ramp), with 5.5a (role substrate + enforcement spine) fixed first. **Roadmap:** 5.5a `useMyProjectRoles` bulk hook + Per-Project Home access gate + Portfolio role-filter (no-op offline) + break contractor Plan/Observe equivalence (403) -> 5.5b team-member assignment-scoped Per-Project Home -> 5.5c contractor task-only view + data-layer query scoping -> 5.5d landowner read-only progress view (on the presentation/portal substrate) + contractor access expiry (task-complete / manual / 90-day). Hook signature unchanged ÔÇö the one surviving piece of the original carry-over. **Verified:** design-only (no tsc / vitest / preview); spec self-review passed (no placeholders, internally consistent, scoped, sole ambiguity ÔÇö contractor enforcement mechanism ÔÇö explicitly deferred to the 5.5a plan); `git diff --cached --name-only` confirmed exactly 4 wiki files staged (ADR + this log entry + index.md + log.md pointers), no foreign WIP from the exclusion list. **Immediate next:** Slice 5.5a implementation plan + execution; 5.5b-d each depend on 5.5a's substrate. ADR [[decisions/2026-05-28-atlas-scoped-views-epic-design]]; continues [[log/2026-05-28-per-project-home-slice54]]; no-deletion; 3-item nav forward IA ([[project-lifecycle-retirement]]); CSRA model untouched; ASCII-only copy.

Shipped Phase 5 Slice 5.4 of the OLOS UX spec as a single explicit-path commit: the canonical **Per-Project Home** mounted at **both** `/v3/project/$projectId/home` (canonical landing) **and** `/v3/project/$projectId/` (default project route, no `home` suffix) so deep links and the default landing converge on the same `PerProjectHomePage` component, replacing the legacy `V3HomePage` mount on `v3IndexRoute`+`v3HomeRoute` (V3HomePage preserved on disk + import per [[feedback-no-deletion]] for Phase 7 retirement). The surface is composed of three regions per the Slice 5.3 ADR carry-over contract: **NextUpCard** (priority router that walks `urgency.breakdown` channels in descending severity ÔÇö draft wizard ÔåÆ "Resume the project wizard" / critical divergence ÔåÆ "1 critical field divergence to review" ÔåÆ high divergence ÔåÆ "N field divergences to review" ÔåÆ stale foundation ÔåÆ "N foundation domains need fresh data" ÔåÆ cyclical review due ÔåÆ "Decision review due" ÔåÆ blocked field actions ÔåÆ field action fallback via `getNextUpForProject` ÔåÆ "Nothing urgent ÔÇö land is steady." with no CTA), **AttentionRail** (vertical chip list keyed off the shared `buildUrgencyChips(urgency)` helper, one chip per non-zero breakdown channel ÔÇö excluding `draftWizard` which is rendered as a separate "Finish setup" pill in the header ÔÇö with empty state "No urgent signals. Land is steady."), and **StageStatusRow** (three `BentoBox` cards summarising Plan tier objective status via `computeAllObjectiveStatuses(PLAN_TIER_OBJECTIVES, toProgressMap(progress))`, field action counts via `useFieldActionStore.byProject[projectId]`, and foundation domain freshness via `computeDomainFreshness(points, nowMs, OBSERVE_DOMAIN_CATALOG[d].freshnessThresholds)` over `FOUNDATION_DOMAINS_FOR_REVISION` ÔÇö Hydrology, Soil, Risk). The composing **`useProjectUrgency([project])`** hook from Slice 5.3 is consumed in **single-project mode** ÔÇö the hook handles arbitrary array lengths with referentially-stable `Map<projectId, ProjectUrgencyResult>` returns, so the one-element case requires zero new substrate; the page reads `urgencyMap.get(project.id)` and threads `urgency` into NextUpCard + AttentionRail while StageStatusRow reads producer stores directly (it is not an urgency consumer). The urgency score is **never rendered** anywhere on the surface ÔÇö NextUpCard uses it only as a structural tie-break inside its priority router (and even then the router orders branches by severity first, so the score rarely load-bears), AttentionRail surfaces breakdown channels as chips, StageStatusRow surfaces producer state directly; three roles, one canonical urgency reader, one canonical chip helper. The shared **`buildUrgencyChips` helper** was extracted from Slice 5.3's inlined `buildChips` into `apps/web/src/v3/home/urgencyChips.ts` so Portfolio Home and Per-Project Home cannot drift in copy or tone assignment as the urgency breakdown shape evolves; `ProjectUrgencyCard` adopts the helper (deletes 83 lines of inlined chip logic + types, adds the import + same rendering ÔÇö rendered markup byte-identical to Slice 5.3 by construction). Surface = the shared stage-agnostic `CommandCentreShell` (Observe/Plan/Act); `.shell` grid (`auto minmax(0,1fr) auto`) is the sole direct child of AppShell's `.main` (`flex:1; position:relative; overflow:hidden`). **Root cause ÔÇö two facts in `.shell` combined:** (1) `height:100%` didn't reliably bound the grid against the positioned `.main`, so it rendered auto-height and the `1fr` body row stretched to the **tallest column** (Act's tall right ops rail), pushing the `auto` tray row below the viewport where `.main{overflow:hidden}` clipped the cards ÔÇö worst on All Modules/Tracker (tallest rail; the carousel is horizontal, so item count *widens* not *heightens*). (2) No explicit grid **column** ÔåÆ implicit `auto` column grew to the widest row's max-content (long carousel/tab strip), ballooning the body to ~9710px and shoving the rail off-screen (latent horizontal blowout). **Fix (CSS-only, `.shell`):** `height:100%`ÔåÆ`position:absolute; inset:0` (definite height ÔåÆ grid clamps, sidebar/rail scroll internally, tray always visible) + add `grid-template-columns: minmax(0,1fr)` (pins rows to viewport width; inner `overflow:auto` scrolls within its box). One shared sheet fixes all three stages uniformly; purely presentational (no JSX/store/schema/model/migration ÔÇö covenant-clean). **Verified:** live DOM (`preview_eval`) shell bounded 812px (=`.main` height), body 1416 with sidebar 268/map 784/rail 340 all on-screen (`railOnScreen:true`, `trayWithinViewport:true`) **+ a confirming screenshot** of the full Act layout incl. intact Tracker cards (per the preview-verification rule ÔÇö captured, not assumed); checked the failing All Modules/Tracker tabs + a low-count tab (no regression). **Process:** an early `git add` swept 61 files (60 pre-existing foreign staged); recovered via `reset --soft HEAD~1` + unstage-all + explicit-path add (final = 1 file), prior index restored. Foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]]; explicit-path commit per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]] (commit survived a later out-of-band rebase [[project-branch-rebase]], reflog-confirmed; HEAD now `f5a4cd94`). - [2026-05-25 ÔÇö Sync-queue circuit-breaker (propagate failures + surface drops)](log/2026-05-25-sync-circuit-breaker.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`84bb8e91`, 5 files +322/ÔêÆ37). Closed the circuit-breaker deferred by [[log/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-fix]]: `flush()`'s retry/backoff/drop machinery only engages when the executor **throws**, but `executeQueuedOp` routed create/update through the *swallowing* live-path handlers (`try { api } catch { warn; enqueue }`) ÔÇö so a failing queued op never incremented `retryCount`, never backed off, and (after the coalescing-key fix) re-enqueued under the same key `flush()` just dequeued ÔåÆ **silently dropped after one pass**. Fix: a `rethrow = false` param on each swallowing create/update handler (`syncProject/Zone/Structure/Path/Utility Create/Update`, `syncProjectBoundary`, generic `typedCreate`/`typedUpdate`) re-throws before the re-enqueue; `executeQueuedOp` create/update now pass `true` (delete/state-blob/comment already throw). New `handleExhaustedOp` wired as `flush()`'s new `onDrop` callback ÔåÆ records the dropped key in a new `droppedStores` channel on `connectivityStore` (dedupe, not persisted) + one `toast.error`; `OfflineBanner` gets a new highest-severity "could not be saved ÔÇö kept on this device" banner with dismissable chips. Live path unchanged (default `rethrow=false`). Verified: typecheck exit 0; new `syncServiceCircuitBreaker.test.ts` (6) + 123 existing sync tests green. **Phase 2 static audit:** the dormant full-coverage path behind `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` (off by default) is fully wired + unit-verified (129/129) ÔÇö classification/guard, flag-gated push+pull, 409 never-clobber, version-skew guard; flagged `ogden-projects` double-classification (`active-singleton`/`whole` **and** typed `subscribeToProjects`) for the E2E. Deferred (human-gated): two-device E2E + `FEATURE_SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` rollout; `projectBundle.ts` kept (no-deletion). The drop-surfacing is the safety property that makes rollout safe. ADR [[decisions/2026-05-25-atlas-sync-circuit-breaker]]; hardens [[concepts/local-first-architecture]] ahead of [[concepts/full-syncservice-coverage-backlog]].
- [2026-05-25 ÔÇö Sync-queue OOM fix (coalescing key + bounded flush)](log/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-fix.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`e5e8f220`). Fixed recurring Chrome "Out of Memory" crash on command-centre routes. Root cause (confirmed via a "Syncing 254520 changesÔÇª" screenshot, after refuting every in-render hypothesis by measurement): the IndexedDB sync queue was an unbounded append log ÔÇö `enqueue()` keyed ops by random UUID so the same failing entity re-queued forever, and `flush()` loaded the whole queue via `getAll()` (250k ops ├ù GeoJSON = multi-GB) into the JS heap. Fix: coalescing deterministic key `storeType:action:localId` (re-queue overwrites ÔåÆ growth bounded), `getBatch(limit)` cursor read + `FLUSH_BATCH=200` instead of `getAll()`, `reconcile()` one-time cursor collapse run at `syncService.start()`, and `flush()` now drops exhausted ops. Verified: 20k-op runaway reconciled to 5 with heap flat ~71ÔÇô74 MB then drained to 0; typecheck exit 0. Deferred: circuit-breaker for the ~14 swallow-and-re-enqueue executor handlers. ADR [[decisions/2026-05-25-sync-queue-oom-coalescing-fix]]; hardens [[concepts/local-first-architecture]].

- [2026-05-25 ÔÇö fix(ops): OLOS login "Failed to fetch" ÔÇö API down + DB behind](log/2026-05-25-fix-olos-login-failed-to-fetch.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Operational fix, **no source changes**. Login showed `TypeError: Failed to fetch`; root cause = the Fastify **API was not running on 3001** (`ECONNREFUSED`), so the Vite proxy (`/api` ÔåÆ `localhost:3001`) had nothing to forward to. Raw "Failed to fetch" (not the proxy's friendly `503 API_OFFLINE`) because the browser tab was on a **dead origin** ÔÇö standard web port 5200 was also down (only a `web-5201` parallel session was live); a no-response fetch makes `apiClient` re-throw the raw error (`apps/web/src/lib/apiClient.ts:156-170`). **Red herring:** `docker exec ogden-postgres psql` showed the DB at migration 037 while `pnpm migrate` (over `DATABASE_URL`ÔåÆ`localhost:5432`) showed 042 ÔÇö because a **native `postgresql-x64-17` Windows service** owns `localhost:5432` (the DB the API uses) and the docker `ogden-postgres` container is stale + shadowed; documented in [[entities/database]] (always check DB state over TCP, never `docker exec`). **Fix:** applied pending migrations (`042_fix_farm_project_type` clean), started API (clean boot, PG+Redis connected, `/health` 200), started web on 5200. **Verified:** in-browser `fetch('/api/v1/auth/login')` with bad creds ÔåÆ real `401 UNAUTHORIZED "Invalid email or password"` (no more "Failed to fetch"). The proxy's `API_OFFLINE` 503 only protects users on a *live* origin; a stale tab / offline-PWA cache (`FEATURE_OFFLINE=true`) on a dead origin still shows raw "Failed to fetch" ÔÇö flagged, not changed.

- [2026-05-25 ÔÇö Blob-sync ramp Stage 1: real-Postgres validation surfaces two flip-blocking bugs](log/2026-05-25-blobsync-stage1-validation-two-latent-bugs.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`, commit `e6b48857` (2 files, +20/ÔêÆ4). First run of `blobSync.integration` (cases A/B/C) against a **live Postgres** for Stage 1 of the `FLAGS.SYNC_STATE_BLOBS` ramp ÔÇö caught two latent `/project-state` route bugs the FIFO-mock suites cannot see. **(1)** `rev` (`BIGINT`) comes back from postgres.js as a **string**, failing `ProjectStateBlob.parse` (`z.number`) ÔåÆ **422 on every successful PUT**; coerced in `parseRow`. **(2)** the PUT pre-stringified then cast `::jsonb`, **double-encoding** the payload into a jsonb string scalar (`jsonb_typeof = string`); the client does no `JSON.parse` so hydration would load stores with a string ÔÇö fixed with `${db.json(...)}::jsonb` (serialize once). Also fixed the spec's project INSERTs to supply `org_id` (NOT NULL since migration 036) by resolving the register-time personal org. Infra: the compose container on 5432 was shadowed by a host-native PG17 on IPv4 5432, sidestepped via a throwaway `postgis:16-3.4` on **5433** (fresh volume ÔåÆ auto-migrate), torn down after. Verified: integration **A/B/C 3/3** real Postgres; mock `projectState` 6/6 + `vegetationSuccession` 8/8 (no regression); `@ogden/api` `tsc` exit 0. **Ramp impact:** the flag was **not flip-ready** before `e6b48857`; Stage 1 gate now green, Stages 2 (operator matrix), 3 (soak), 4 (flip) remain gated. Explicit-path commit, foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]]. Follows [[log/2026-05-25-versioned-blob-skip-dev-observability]].

- [2026-05-25 ÔÇö Compass toast reads real How-checks, not seed evidence](log/2026-05-25-compass-toast-reads-real-checks.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`73ff75a0`, 3 files). See ADR [[2026-05-25-atlas-compass-toast-reads-real-checks]]. Steward screenshot bug: the Observe **HUMAN CONTEXT** panel read **"33% ┬À 1/3 steps"** (only the last How checkbox ticked) yet the in-map **"Objective complete"** toast fired ÔÇö "Just because the last task on the list is marked complete it renders the whole objective as complete." Chose to fix **all three stages** (AskUserQuestion). **Root cause:** two parallel progress systems read different sources ÔÇö the visible panel (`GuidanceCard` via `*ChecklistAside`) uses `progressFromChecks(checked, how.length)` over the **real** per-stage How-checks store (ÔåÆ1/3 Ô£ô), but the toast (`*ObjectiveCompletePrompt` via the single-objective hooks `use*ObjectiveProgress`) used `objectiveProgress` over the **seed-backed compass** store, where `isVerified = raw[i]==='verified' || checked.includes(i)`; the Observe `human-context` SEED `{0:'verified',1:'verified',2:'evidence-in'}` + the one real tick on node 2 = 3/3 = 100% ÔåÆ false toast. Purely SEED-as-completion, not a count mismatch (`nodes.length === how.length` since compass nodes are `how.map(...)`). **Fix (3 files, ÔêÆ12 net):** repoint each single-objective hook (`useCompassData.ts`/`usePlanCompassData.ts`/`useActCompassData.ts`) to `progressFromChecks(checks ?? EMPTY_CHECKS, obj.nodes.length)`, dropping the `seedFor` evidence read + `evidence` dep; compass-store imports stay (the plural `use*CompassData` **wheel** hook still uses SEED for its prototype). - [2026-05-25 ÔÇö Compass progress fill: outside-in (rim ÔåÆ centre)](log/2026-05-25-compass-progress-fill-outside-in.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** atlas `feat/atlas-permaculture` (`d181f223`, 2 files) + `ogden-ui-components` `release/v0.1.1`/tag `v0.1.1` (`e71fcc3`). Steward, looking at the **True North** compass, asked each progress wedge to **fill from the outer rim inward toward the hub** as completion rises (full wedge at 100%, sliver at the rim near 0%), reversing the prior centreÔåÆrim fill. **The non-obvious part: the wheel isn't in atlas.** It's the shared `MaqasidComparisonWheel` in the separate repo `@ogden/ui-components`, consumed as a **pinned GitHub tarball** whose `dist/` is **committed** ÔÇö so the fix is a cross-repo release: edit source + rebuild/commit `dist/` in the component repo, then bump atlas's pin. **Steward decisions (AskUserQuestion):** (a) **surgical patch v0.1.1** off the `v0.1.0` tag (avoids pulling intervening additive BBOS/educational components into atlas); (b) **all wheels** ÔÇö flip once in the shared component, no opt-in prop. **The change = 3 lines, one file:** the existing `annularSector(rInner, rOuter,ÔÇª)` helper already takes both radii, so progress flips from a *moving outer* radius (`currentR = HUB_R + (PROGRESS_MAX_R-HUB_R)┬Àpct`) to a *moving inner* radius (`fillInnerR = PROGRESS_MAX_R - (PROGRESS_MAX_R-HUB_R)┬Àpct`; `HUB_R=56`, `PROGRESS_MAX_R=142`), with the `mcw-seg-current` fill + `mcw-seg-pattern` overlay drawn as `annularSector(fillInnerR, PROGRESS_MAX_R,ÔÇª)`. Dim track / 0%-empty ring / complete-arc / gradient / entrance animation untouched ÔÇö **no CSS change**. **Blast radius = 5 atlas surfaces** (True North, Observe, Plan, Act, OPA dashboard wheel); the separate `CycleWheel` is out of scope. **Release+pin:** branched from `v0.1.0`, `npm run build` regenerated dist, committed source+dist (`e71fcc3`), tagged+pushed; atlas pin `#v0.1.0`ÔåÆ`#v0.1.1` (root `package.json` only; `apps/web` doesn't pin), `corepack pnpm install` ÔåÆ lockfile resolves `e71fcc3`. **Verification:** `preview_screenshot` times out (MapLibre/WebGL, **stated not claimed**); verified by a deterministic geometry probe of the **installed** minified bundle ÔÇö fill resolves to `a = H - (H - B)┬À(i/100)` with `H=142`/`B=56` and the path call `annularSector(a, H,ÔÇª)`, i.e. outer pinned at 142, inner tracks pct (142 at 0% ÔåÆ 56 at 100%); conclusive since geometry is a pure fn of pct. Atlas staged by **explicit path** (`package.json`+`pnpm-lock.yaml`), foreign WIP untouched per [[feedback-no-deletion]], divergence-checked before push per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]. **Addendum ÔÇö "wheel looks unchanged" root cause + forward-port:** the steward then reported the wheel looked the same; investigation found the code was correct but the app **served stale pixels** ÔÇö (1) the **v0.1.1 release never bumped `package.json` `version`** (stuck at `0.1.0`), so caches had no invalidation signal *(the real defect)*, and (2) atlas's `optimizeDeps.exclude` serves the dep raw and vite **doesn't watch `node_modules`**, so the dev server running since before the install kept its old transform. **Fix:** restart the dev server + clear `apps/web/node_modules/.vite`; DOM-probe then confirmed outer arc fixed at 142 / inner tracks pct = rimÔåÆcentre (`preview_screenshot` times out on WebGL, stated not claimed). **Lesson:** *a release must bump `package.json` `version`, not just move a tag.* **Forward-port done:** same 3-line flip applied to `ogden-ui-components` `main`, `version` bumped 0.3.0ÔåÆ**0.3.1** (defect not repeated), dist rebuilt (diff limited to the `index` bundles + maps), committed by explicit path, **tagged `v0.3.1`**, pushed (`46a1815..90aa7c6`). v0.1.1 left intact; atlas pin-to-v0.3.1 noted as non-blocking follow-up. **Addendum ÔÇö atlas pin bumped v0.1.1 ÔåÆ v0.3.1 (`77fe24af`):** closed that follow-up ÔÇö pin `#v0.1.1`ÔåÆ`#v0.3.1` so atlas now carries the **correct `version` field** (0.3.1), closing the cache-busting defect; same wheel geometry, plus additive BBOS/educational (zero bundle impact ÔÇö atlas imports only the wheel/hover-store/LevelNavigator, BBOS is a separate dist entry). **The gotcha:** v0.3.x changed the dist from single-file (`dist/ogden-ui-components.es.js`) to **multi-entry** (`dist/index.es.js` + `dist/bbos.es.js`), and atlas resolves via a hardcoded **vite alias** (not the `exports` map), so the alias was repointed `dist/ogden-ui-components.es.js`ÔåÆ`dist/index.es.js` (CSS alias unchanged ÔÇö same filename). **Verified:** installed `version` = 0.3.1; - [2026-05-24 ÔÇö MapLibre marker hover fix + temporary Command Centre unlock](log/2026-05-24-marker-hover-fix-and-command-centre-unlock.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Two small compass/map touch-ups. **(1) Bug fix `80f2b9d3`:** hovering a Command Centre objective marker made it jump to the map's top-left corner. Root cause ÔÇö MapLibre writes the *entire* positioning `transform` (`translate(-50%,-50%) translate(x,y)ÔÇª`) onto a DOM marker's own element each frame; the `mouseenter` handler set `el.style.transform = 'scale(...)'` on that **same** element, erasing the translate ÔåÆ marker snapped to the container origin until the next position write. Fix: move the hover scale to an inner `pin` child (`line-height:0` outer shrink-wraps it; geometry unchanged, clicks bubble); fixed in both `ObjectiveMapMarkers.tsx` (reported) and `FieldFlagOverlay.tsx` (identical pattern). Other DOM-marker overlays don't hover-transform (grep-verified). **Reusable lesson: never write `transform` on a MapLibre marker element ÔÇö scale an inner child.** **(2) Temp unlock `e615c6da`:** steward asked to enter the Observe Command Centre without all objectives verified; the center-unlock gate ([[decisions/2026-05-24-atlas-observe-command-centre]]) is one `ready` flag in `StageCompassPage.tsx` driving the wheel hotspot's clickability + `forceConverged` glow + `onEnter()`. Forced `ready = data.views.length > 0`, marked **TEMP** with the exact one-line revert in a comment. Both pure presentation/behaviour ÔÇö covenant clean, no schema/store/model/migration. `tsc` at the 3-error pre-existing baseline; committed by name per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]]; live preview not run (MapLibre canvas hangs screenshots ÔÇö documented standard).

- [2026-05-22 ÔÇö Plan/Observe follow-ups: maplibre line-width fix + URL-persist picked section](log/2026-05-22-plan-observe-followups-linewidth-url-persist.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closed the two deferred follow-ups from [[log/2026-05-22-cross-rail-single-section-highlight]] (`fc0938b8`). **Part 1 ÔÇö `design-el-line` line-width** (`apps/web/src/v3/plan/canvas/layers/DesignElementLayers.tsx`): the layer threw `paint.line-width: Only one zoom-based "step" or "interpolate" subexpression may be used` **every frame**, because a zoom-based `lineWidthExpr` was nested inside a `case` **and** referenced twice (`['case', selFlag, ['+', lineWidthExpr, 2], lineWidthExpr]`) ÔÇö two nested zoom curves. MapLibre requires the zoom curve to be the **outermost** expression of a paint property (only the *input* must be `['zoom']`; feature-state is allowed in stop *outputs*). Fix: collapsed to a **single top-level** zoom `interpolate` with the `selFlag` `+2px` selection delta folded into each stop output; dropped the `case` wrap. Console buffer now clean of the error. **Part 2 ÔÇö URL-persist `?section=`** (`PlanLayout.tsx` + `ObserveLayout.tsx`): moved `activeSectionId` from per-Layout `useState` to a URL **search param** (`useSearch({ strict:false }) as { section?: string }`), so the single-section cross-rail highlight survives reloads/back-forward/shared links. **No `validateSearch`** added ÔÇö matches the `ObserveDeepLinkFocus` convention and avoids stripping the existing `focus*` deep-link params. Navigation collapsed into one `navigateModuleSection(mod, sectionId)` primitive writing the `$module` path + `?section` atomically (`navigate`'s `search` *replaces*, so passed explicitly every time); `handleSelectModule`ÔåÆ`(mod,null)` (whole family), `handleSelectSection` toggles on strict identity; PlanLayout's silvopasture-drilldown effect navigate also got `search:{}`. The four rail components are unchanged (already consume `effectiveSectionId`+`onSelectSection`). **Verification:** `cd apps/web && npm run typecheck` at the **3-error pre-existing baseline** (`StepBoundary.tsx`, two `HostUnion*` tests); live DOM/URL evals (:5200) ÔÇö Plan cold-load `?section=be-agricultural`ÔåÆ2 active (survives reload), click narrows+writes `?section`, click active deselects+drops module&section (0), no-sectionÔåÆfamily (10); Observe `?section=be-building`ÔåÆ2, `be-from-map`ÔåÆ1 (main rail only, documented), no-sectionÔåÆfamily (13), live click writes `?section`. **Screenshot blocker root-cause corrected:** the prior session blamed the line-width error for the `preview_screenshot` 30 s timeout ÔÇö **wrong.** With the error gone the screenshot still times out because the preview tab is **backgrounded** (`document.visibilityState==='hidden'`, `hasFocus()===false`), which throttles `requestAnimationFrame` so any frame-dependent op hangs while synchronous evals return instantly; `preview_resize` didn't foreground it. So the blocker is an **environment** condition (preview pane not focused), not renderer saturation and not the line-width bug ÔÇö stated not assumed per the preview-verification rule; synchronous DOM/URL evals are authoritative here. Staged only the 3 files by explicit path; foreign WIP (EconomicsPanel, capitalPartner, SectorCompassOverlay, ZoneSomSidebar) untouched per `feedback_no_deletion`. Plan: `~/.claude/plans/the-sector-compass-in-memoized-sphinx.md`.

Closes the last gap from [the sources-wired session](log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sources-wired.md): the `client_error_events` sink has **four** `source` values and the fourth, **`api_client`**, was still dark ÔÇö API failures surfaced only as thrown `ApiError`s + uncaught network rejections, invisible server-side. **Scope (operator-confirmed):** report **all** failures (every `ApiError` incl. 401, **and** network/offline `fetch` rejections as `status:0`/`code:'NETWORK_ERROR'`, re-thrown unchanged); always-on **loop guard** excludes `/api/v1/telemetry/*` so a failed client-errors POST can't report itself; deliberate `AbortError`s skipped. **`apiClient.ts`** gains reporter-injection plumbing mirroring `setSessionExpiredHandler` (`ApiClientErrorReport` + `setApiClientErrorReporter` + private `reportApiFailure`); `request()` now wraps `fetch` in try/catch (reports non-abort rejections, re-throws original) and reports at the `ApiError` throw site before throwing. **Bundle-split preserved** ÔÇö apiClient does **not** import `clientErrorLog` (would cycle, since clientErrorLog imports `api`, and drag the buffer into always-mounted code per [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]]); instead **`bootAuthed.ts`** (authed-only) registers the bridge `setApiClientErrorReporter((r) => recordClientError({ source:'api_client', ... }))`, `projectId` omitted so the active-project resolver stamps it. `stack`/`details` deliberately omitted (uninformative / payload-lean / no body leak). **Tests:** new `apiClient.clientError.test.ts` (happy-dom, stubbed `fetch`, spy reporter) ÔÇö 6/6 green (5xx reported, 401 reported, network reported+rethrown, AbortError not reported, loop guard, no-reporter safe); web tsc shows only the 3 pre-existing unrelated baseline errors. **Follow-up (same day, commits `82d2bb19` code + `0f86be26` wiki):** the two upload throw sites are now wired too ÔÇö `files.upload` (XHR) gains a `fail()` helper reporting each `ApiError` reject site (non-2xx `onload`, parse `catch`, `onerror`), and `regenerationEvents.uploadMedia` (fetch) became `async` with the same try/catch-around-fetch + report-before-throw pattern as `request()`; 4 new test cases (XHR stub + fetch mock) ÔåÆ 10/10 green, tsc baseline unchanged. **Every API failure path now emits `api_client` telemetry ÔÇö no dark paths remain.** ADR back-links: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]], [[log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sources-wired]].

- [2026-05-21 ÔÇö Client-error telemetry: react_error_boundary + unhandled_rejection wired, migration 039 applied](log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sources-wired.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Direct follow-up to [the client-error telemetry sink](log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sink.md), which shipped `recordClientError` + the buffered POST pipeline + the `client_error_events` table but left three of its four `source` enum values unused. This session wires the **two highest-value remaining sources** and applies the table migration. **`react_error_boundary`** ÔÇö both error boundaries in `apps/web/src/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx` (generic `ErrorBoundary` + always-mounted `GlobalErrorBoundary`) now call a shared `reportBoundaryError(error, info, boundary)` from `componentDidCatch`, emitting `source:'react_error_boundary'` with `context.boundary` + a 4000-char-capped `componentStack`. Because `GlobalErrorBoundary` mounts on every path incl. `/showcase/*`, the helper uses a **lazy `import('../lib/clientErrorLog.js')`** to keep the authed graph out of the showcase initial chunk ([[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]]). **`unhandled_rejection`** ÔÇö new `apps/web/src/lib/globalErrorHandlers.ts` (`installGlobalErrorHandlers()`) registers one idempotent `window.unhandledrejection` listener; it statically imports `clientErrorLog`, so it is imported **only from `bootAuthed.ts`** (authed-only ÔÇö showcase ships no client-error telemetry). `window.onerror` deliberately out of scope (no matching enum source; React render errors already covered). **projectId resolver** ÔÇö `clientErrorLog.ts` gains `setClientErrorProjectIdResolver(fn)`; `recordClientError` uses `input.projectId !== undefined ? input.projectId : safeResolveProjectId()` so an explicit value (incl. the persist helper's explicit `null`) wins, an omitted one falls back to the resolver (`bootAuthed.ts` registers `() => useProjectStore.getState().activeProjectId ?? null`); `safeResolveProjectId` swallows resolver throws. **Migration 039 applied to the LOCAL DEV DB** ÔÇö investigation confirmed there is **no prod/staging DB** (staging parked, [[log/2026-04-21-staging-provisioning-decision-parked]]); only local dev Postgres exists, operator confirmed. Runner applies all pending in order (can't target one), so 039 + additive 040/041 (`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS`, verified non-destructive) applied together via `node --env-file=.env --import=tsx src/db/migrate.ts`. Verified `client_error_events`: 14 cols, nullable `project_id`/`stack`, 2 indexes, 4-source CHECK constraint; `039` in `schema_migrations`. **Tests:** new `globalErrorHandlers.test.ts` (3) + `ErrorBoundary.telemetry.test.tsx` (3) + extended `clientErrorLog.test.ts` resolver block (3) ÔÇö 20 targeted tests green; web tsc shows only the 3 pre-existing unrelated errors. Commit `2eb2aa6a` (frontend slice). **Remaining gap:** `api_client` is the last unwired source (deferred ÔÇö lower value). ADR back-links: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-bundle-split]], [[log/2026-05-21-client-error-telemetry-sink]].
- [2026-05-21 ÔÇö Phase 5 (Slice B): Showcase observation loop](log/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-5-observation.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. The final phase of the Apricot-Lane-inspired Showcase Program ÔÇö adds the observation loop the public `/showcase/three-streams` portal ([[log/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-3-showcase-portal]]) shipped without. Two blockers: the authed telemetry pipeline (`POST /api/v1/telemetry/act-interactions` + `act_interaction_events`) is `authenticate`-gated and its `user_id`/`project_id` are both NOT NULL ÔÇö a cold showcase visitor is anonymous by definition. **Decision: a parallel anonymous-first path, not a relaxed authed one** ([[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-observation-loop]]); the authed pipeline is left untouched. **Quantitative half** ÔÇö migration `040_showcase_visitor_events.sql` (`bb54a4fb`) inverts the NOT-NULL invariants (nullable `user_id`/`project_id`; `session_id` the cross-event handle; `event_type` CHECK on 7 lifecycle events; `tier` CHECK NULL-or-enum; idempotent) + PUBLIC rate-limited (`60/min`) `POST /api/v1/telemetry/showcase-events` with best-effort `jwtVerify` (stamps `user_id` only if a bearer happens to be present) and best-effort per-event bulk insert (`cbe90535`). **Client wiring** (`57de13f8`) ÔÇö `showcaseEventLog.ts` mirrors `actInteractionLog.ts`'s batcher shape but POSTs via plain `fetch` + `navigator.sendBeacon` with type-only `@ogden/shared` imports (keeps the Phase 3.5 lean SSG bundle free of `authStore`/`projectStore`/Cesium); instruments `TierChooser`/`ContactCTA`/route-mount/register/instantiate. **Qualitative half** ÔÇö migration `041_showcase_feedback.sql` + PUBLIC `POST /api/v1/telemetry/showcase-feedback` + `FeedbackForm.tsx` mounted between `<ContactCTA>` and `<AttributionFooter>` (`051518e9`); `message` the one required field (client + route trim + DB CHECK backstop), `rating`/`contact` opt-in, reads (not creates) the telemetry `session_id` to cross-link, deliberately ungated by `VITE_ATLAS_TELEMETRY_ENABLED` (explicit submission is opt-in, not passive telemetry). **Covenant ratchet** (`f3a5aeb8`) ÔÇö `covenant.test.ts`'s `git ls-files` subtree scan pulled both new files in scope automatically; one catch-and-fix where the `FeedbackForm` docstring *enumerated* the forbidden tokens and tripped the ratchet on its own prose (reworded). **Privacy posture:** anonymous by default (ephemeral `sessionStorage` id, no cookie/fingerprint/PII), the only PII channel (`showcase_feedback.contact`) is opt-in, cross-link not identity; consent banner deferred (documented in ADR). Gate: API tsc exit 0; web tsc 0 new errors above baseline; showcase vitest green incl. covenant ratchet + Apricot Lane exact-string. **Program complete** (Phase 0 ÔåÆ 5). ADR back-links: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-showcase-observation-loop]], [[entities/showcase-portal]], [[log/2026-05-21-atlas-phase-2.5-livestock-seed]].

- [2026-05-21 ÔÇö Phase G hotfix: Vite alias for `@ogden/shared/evidence`](log/2026-05-21-phase-g-vite-alias-hotfix.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Unblocks dev-server boot after Phase G G.1 added `./evidence` to `packages/shared/package.json` exports but did not update the parallel `resolve.alias` map in `apps/web/vite.config.ts`. Symptom: Vite v6.4.1 returned HTTP 500 on `DecisionTriad.tsx` / `LandVerdictCard.tsx` / `auditEmit.ts` with "Failed to resolve import `@ogden/shared/evidence`"; React root never mounted. Root cause: `vite.config.ts:172-196` carries an explicit alias map for every `@ogden/shared/*` subpath because Vite's dev-server cwd is `apps/web/` and cannot traverse up to the workspace-root node_modules; the bare `@ogden/shared` entry prefix-matched any unaliased subpath and rewrote it to `packages/shared/src/index.ts/evidence` (nonsense). Node's resolver was happy (verified via `require.resolve`); Vite's alias-first chain short-circuited before reaching the exports field. Fix: one-line add at `apps/web/vite.config.ts:194` ÔÇö `'@ogden/shared/evidence': resolve(__dirname, '../../packages/shared/src/evidence/index.ts')` ÔÇö placed before the bare-package fallback per the "more-specific first" rule in the surrounding comment. Verification: all three modules HTTP 200; `apps/web` typecheck clean for evidence code (3 pre-existing unrelated errors untouched: `StepBoundary.tsx`, `HostUnionContextMenu.test.tsx`, `HostUnionDrilldownCard.test.tsx`). Lesson: future subpath additions to `packages/shared/package.json` exports **must also** add the matching `vite.config.ts` alias entry ÔÇö the two surfaces are parallel and Vite's prefix-match silently fails for any apps/web consumer otherwise.

- [2026-05-21 ÔÇö Click-delete vertex fix (onMouseUp ÔåÆ onClick)](log/2026-05-21-click-delete-vertex-fix.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Bug-fix for user-reported "clicking on a vertex does not remove it" in real Chrome. Root cause: `clickDeleteDirectSelect.ts` attached deletion to `onMouseUp`, but MapboxDraw's `events.mouseup` routes click-gestures (`isClick`: Ôëñ 4 px / Ôëñ 500 ms) to `currentMode.onClick`, drag-releases to `currentMode.onMouseUp` ÔÇö so plain vertex clicks never reached the delete branch. Two slices: **`90fef60a`** moved deletion to `onClick`, dropped the now-redundant in-mode pixel-threshold (MapboxDraw's own `isClick` already gates), and returns early without delegating to `stock.onClick` when the min-vertex guard fires (otherwise `clickActiveFeature` clears `selectedCoordPaths` and kicks the user out of vertex-edit on the 3rd vertex of a triangle); also resets `_cdVertexCoordPath` on every `onMouseDown`. **`16dc2d79`** appended a corrective "later" section to the [partial smoke-walk log](log/2026-05-21-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete.md) striking through its "harness limitation" framing ÔÇö the harness was a red herring layered on top of a real regression. Typecheck exit 0. Real-browser keystroke confirmation of the remaining smoke-walk steps still owed. Branch hygiene: stashed unrelated parallel-session edits (basemap-water-adoption + template_slug migration) before commit, restored after push; `git fetch` 2/0 before push; FF clean.

- [2026-05-21 ÔÇö Observe-anno "stuck source" diagnosis closed as headless-RAF artefact](log/2026-05-21-observe-anno-sources-false-alarm.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. **No code change.** Wiki-only documentation closing the "four observe-anno sources never reach `loaded:true`" investigation as not-a-bug. Live preview verification at `/v3/project/mtc/observe` with two seeded Conventional Crop polygons shows `m.isSourceLoaded('observe-anno-conventional-crop') === true` and `queryRenderedFeatures` returning the crop with correct `annoKind`/`annoId` props ÔÇö after exactly one `_render()` tick. The prior session's "render loop is dead" conclusion was a property-name miss: it probed `m._frame`, but MapLibre 5.x renamed that field to `_frameRequest` and now schedules frames via `AbortController` + `browser.frameAsync` ([`node_modules/maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl-dev.js:57944`](../node_modules/maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl-dev.js)). Re-probing the correct field shows a frame IS queued ÔÇö it just never resolves while the Claude Preview tab is backgrounded (headless Chrome throttles RAF for inactive tabs). All geojson sources show the same idle-paused profile in the preview (`be-v2-*`, `matrix-*-dem`, `design-el-extrusion`, `diagnose-parcel-boundary`), not just the named four; the "siblings load normally" framing in the brief was a probe-timing artefact. **Diagnostic technique worth keeping:** when debugging "isSourceLoaded never true" under Claude Preview, force a paint via `m._render(performance.now())` from the eval console to drain `_updatedSources` and resume paused SourceCaches synchronously enough to read a real state. **Implication for the [vertex-edit + click-delete smoke walk](log/2026-05-21-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete.md):** if "clicks don't open detail panels" reproduces in a real browser, the cause is not stuck sources ÔÇö likelier suspects are `SelectionFloater` consuming the click before the layer handler, the 50 ms `consumedAt` deduper in `ObserveAnnotationLayers.tsx` mis-rejecting, or the form store's `existingId === id && kind === kind` early-return. Disposition: closed as not-a-bug; future sessions should re-test in a real browser before re-opening this thread.

- [2026-05-21 ÔÇö Observe vertex edit + click-to-delete](log/2026-05-21-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Two commits ÔÇö round 1 `14db482f` adds an "Edit vertices" button to `AnnotationDetailPanel` (gated on `POLYGON_KINDS.has(kind) || LINESTRING_KINDS.has(kind)`; sector arcs and point kinds excluded), routing through `observeSelectionStore.set([{kind,id}]) + setMoveMode(true) + closeStore()` (NOT the local `close` wrapper ÔÇö that clears selection) so the existing `AnnotationVertexEditHandler` path picks up. `conventionalCrop` and `pasture` registered in `POLYGON_KINDS` of `annotationGeometryRegistry` with new `readPolygon` / `writePolygon` cases routing to `useConventionalCropStore.updateConventionalCrop({ geometry })` + `usePastureStore.updatePasture({ geometry })`. Round 2 `bcd5e0ad` adds **click-to-delete vertex** via a new `clickDeleteDirectSelect.ts` custom MapboxDraw mode that spreads `MapboxDraw.modes.direct_select` and overrides four lifecycle methods: `onMouseDown` stashes cursor screen-point; `onVertex` captures `coord_path`; `onMidpoint` clears the capture (midpoint click adds a vertex ÔÇö stock behaviour, must not delete the freshly-added one); `onMouseUp` arbitrates click-vs-drag via `Math.hypot(dx, dy) > CLICK_PIXEL_THRESHOLD` (4 px). Click on vertex with capture intact ÔåÆ `feature.removeCoordinate(path)` + `map.fire('draw.update', { features: [feature.toGeoJSON()] })`, which `SharedVertexEditHandler.onUpdate` already consumes ÔÇö no persistence changes. Min-vertex guard `canRemoveCoordinate(feature, coordPath)`: polygons require `ring.length > 4` (closed-ring triangle = 4 entries), lines require `coords.length > 2`. Silent refusal per user choice ÔÇö no toast. `SharedVertexEditHandler.tsx` registers the mode on the per-mount `MapboxDraw` instance and switches `changeMode` from `'direct_select'` to `CLICK_DELETE_DIRECT_SELECT`; Plan-stage `PlanVertexEditHandler` inherits for free via composition. **Behaviour.** Click vertex (no drag) ÔåÆ vertex deleted; click+drag ÔåÆ moves (unchanged); midpoint click ÔåÆ adds vertex (unchanged); click vertex on triangle / 2-vertex line ÔåÆ nothing (silently gated); Esc ÔåÆ exits vertex-edit (unchanged); Cmd-Z ÔåÆ restores via store `temporal()` middleware. `draw_polygon` mode for new polygons unaffected. **Verification.** `pnpm --filter @ogden/web typecheck` shows only 3 pre-existing unrelated errors (`StepBoundary.tsx:365`, two `HostUnionÔÇª` test files) ÔÇö none in touched files. Interactive smoke test **not run** ÔÇö API at `localhost:3001` offline (ECONNREFUSED), blocked login on Vite preview; flagged transparently per CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success." **Out of scope.** Bulk vertex delete (shift-click multi-select); toast on min-vertex refusal; click-delete on points (no vertices, repositioned via `AnnotationDragHandler`); sector arc click-delete (uses `AnnotationSectorHandles`, not vertex-edit). ADR: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete]]. Behavioural memory: [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]] (both slices committed the moment typecheck cleared); [[project-branch-rebase]] (fetched + verified no divergence prior to commit).
