- [2026-05-30 ÔÇö B4 tooltip multi-pin (Slice L)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-multi-pin.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice L of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap. Retires the 2026-05-26 single-pin invariant: `pinnedUnion` (single `{ point, entries, hostIds }` object) replaced with `pinnedHosts: Map<string, HostBlock>` keyed by hostId; per-host click toggle, ESC + tap-outside clear ALL pins, single cursor-anchored stack merging pinned (insertion order, `pinned: true`) with hover (filtered by `!pinnedHosts.has`, `pinned: false`). `lastCursorPointRef` freezes the anchor when the cursor leaves canvas with pins active. Gold accent moves from container-level `.tooltip[data-pinned='true']` (border-color) to per-block `.hostBlock[data-pinned='true']` (2px gold left-border + 6px padding-left) so mixed pinned + hover stacks distinguish sticky from hover-along blocks at a glance. `HostBlockEntry` gains `pinned: boolean` (kept off `HostBlockProps` so the raw-data interface stays narrow); scroll-cap derivation moves from `!!pinned` to `entries.some(e => e.pinned)`. `sameHostIdSet()` helper deleted. **Use-case justification.** Roadmap required "design conversation about whether the use case (steward wanting to compare 2+ hosts side-by-side) is real before committing." Consulted **Permaculture Scholar NotebookLM (`5aa3dcf3-ÔÇª`)** ÔÇö unequivocal yes, citing four canonical permaculture design flows requiring simultaneous comparison of overlapping host canopies: (1) **50-year mature-canopy simulation** (spacing for tree A depends on B/C/D's mature spreads in the same frame); (2) **Edge maximization** (Holmgren P11 "Use Edges and Value the Marginal" ÔÇö biodiversity concentrates in spaces *between* canopies; productive edge can't be designed one tree at a time); (3) **Cross-guild ecological aggregation** (N-fixers + dynamic accumulators + insectaries aggregate into coverage or redundancy ÔÇö multi-guild question by definition); (4) **Suntrap / microclimate engineering** (U-shape / horseshoe arrangements creating sheltered microclimates ÔÇö aggregate footprint + continuous shadow evaluated as a unit). Holmgren P8 ("Integrate Rather Than Segregate") underwrites all four. Single-pin was a segregation affordance working against P8. Scholar citations degenerate (~290 references to same handful of snippets ÔÇö known indexer artifact); substantive claims hold independently against any permaculture-design textbook. **Key architectural choices.** `Map<hostId, HostBlock>` for O(1) per-host toggle + insertion-order iteration (newly-pinned at top of pinned section, consistent with 2026-05-27 topmost-first convention). Per-block accent not container-level so mixed stacks communicate sticky vs hover-along visually. `pinned` on `HostBlockEntry` not `HostBlockProps` (display-state, not raw-data payload). Single cursor-anchored stack rather than separate portals per pin (matches "these are the hosts I'm comparing" mental model). ESC + tap-outside clear ALL pins per roadmap recommendation ("get this off my screen" rarely scoped to one host). In-tooltip dismiss button OUT OF SCOPE ÔÇö below Slice K's threshold=4 the tooltip is `pointer-events: none`, can't receive clicks without retiring the 2026-05-25 invariant; Slice M's drill-down surface (interactive by design) can ship it. **Tests.** Migrated test #3 from container-level `pinned` prop to per-entry; scroll-cap tests migrated to entry-level `pinned: true`. New `describe('multi-pin (Slice L)', ...)` with four cases: mixed pinned + hover (only pinned blocks carry data-pinned; root never carries data-pinned), all-pinned stack (every block carries data-pinned; separators between), all-hover stack (no data-pinned anywhere), scrollable regression guard (1 pinned + 3 hover = 4 ÔëÑ threshold ÔçÆ scrollable because `entries.some` predicate, guarding against future tightening to "all pinned"). **Verification.** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers` ÔåÆ 28/28 (24 prior + 4 new). `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` ÔåÆ 288/288 (36 files; +4 over Slice N's 284). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files; pre-existing unrelated errors elsewhere unchanged. Preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree (Vite resolves against worktree-root `node_modules` which doesn't exist) ÔÇö stated explicitly per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success." **Invariants preserved.** Slice K scroll-cap carve-out + tooltip-testid tap-outside exemption; Slice J / I / H; 2026-05-25 `pointer-events: none` in hover mode + pinned-small-stack; 2026-05-27 multi-feature fan-out (each feature toggles independently); 2026-05-28 ESC + tap-outside dismiss (semantics flip from "clear one" to "clear all"); 2026-05-29 / 30 fade machinery (`pinned` rides alongside `phase`); 2026-05-30 Slice N i18n seam (no new strings). **Invariant retired.** 2026-05-26 single-pin explicitly rolled back; ADR remains in wiki as historical context (defensive reasoning correct at the time, design question now answered). **Out of scope.** In-tooltip dismiss button (Slice M's space); pinned-count badge ("­ƒôî N" header indicator ÔÇö additive, defer); per-guild breakdown line inside a block (Slice O rejection deferred this to Slice M); persistence across page reloads (transient UI); keyboard navigation between pinned blocks (accessibility pass); integration tests for `PlanDataLayers` click-toggle Map logic (defer until a regression points at it). Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N + O + L shipped. **Remaining: Slice M** (hover-card drill-down ÔÇö per-block click opens a richer surface listing per-guild breakdowns; depends on L's per-block addressability, which now exists).
- [2026-05-30 ÔÇö B4 per-layer tinted stripe rejection (Slice O ÔÇö second pass)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-per-layer-stripe-rejection.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice O of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap as a **documentation-only rejection** ÔÇö no code change. The roadmap was explicit that this slice "must start with a research/decision step ÔÇª decide whether the stripe is genuinely distinguishable (different surface) or re-introduces the same problem (same concept, different shape). Only then design the implementation, or document the second rejection with fresh reasoning." This slice ships the second-rejection path. **Prior rejections recap.** 2026-05-24 halo viz ADR colored the union halo neutral grey, explicitly rejecting `LAYER_TINT`: *"Neutral grey (not LAYER_TINT) because the union is a per-host aggregate, not a per-layer geometry; layer-tinting would mislead the eye into reading the halo as canopy-layer-specific."* 2026-05-25 hover tooltip ADR carried the reasoning forward to the tooltip stripe: *"the union is a per-host aggregate; layer-tinting would reintroduce the misleading-hue concern 2026-05-24 called out for the halo itself."* Both deferred as "revisit if needed." **Fresh counter-argument considered.** The natural revisit: the halo is on the map (color = layer-data), but the tooltip is a *separate UI surface* with its own visual conventions (already carries a gold "saved overlap" accent ÔÇö a non-data color), so a stripe there would read as "category metadata," not as "this geometry = green-layer." **Why the counter-argument fails on two grounds.** (1) **Visual contiguity.** The tooltip is cursor-anchored adjacent to the halo it describes ÔÇö stewards see them simultaneously. A green stripe next to a grey halo invites the eye to bind "this host = green," propagating the layer-tint association from the *label* onto the halo it labels. The surface boundary doesn't exist for the eye when the surfaces are positionally adjacent; the 2026-05-24 reasoning survives unchanged: the stripe tints the halo's label, which is the same problem one frame downstream. (2) **"Dominant" is the wrong reduction.** A host is in the silvopasture data because it carries *multiple* canopy layers (polyculture by construction). Every available definition of "dominant" elevates one layer above the others ÔÇö biggest area biases toward fast-spreading shrubs, most members biases toward groundcovers, tallest requires schema work (data model doesn't track per-member heights), alphabetical is arbitrary and defensible only as a tie-breaker. Polyculture composition is the load-bearing feature of the model; hiding four-fifths of it behind one layer's color is a model violation, not a presentation choice. **What the steward actually needs (and where it goes).** The existing counts line ÔÇö *"3 guilds ┬À 7 canopy-bearing members"* ÔÇö already surfaces polyculture composition. If at-a-glance per-layer breakdown matters, the right UI is a small list inside the tooltip (e.g. `overstory ├ù2 ┬À midstory ├ù3 ┬À understory ├ù2`), with each layer name in its own tint *as a label, not as a category color for the host as a whole*. **This breakdown is not in scope for Slice O** ÔÇö it overlaps with **Slice M** (hover-card drill-down), where the natural design move is to expand a block into a richer surface that lists per-guild breakdowns. Whoever picks Slice M up next can lean on this ADR's reasoning to justify the breakdown approach. **Status flip.** 2026-05-24 / 25 ADRs left this as "deferred ÔÇö revisit if needed." This slice flips it to **decided rejection**. Future roadmap sweeps should not re-list it as candidate work without the underlying constraint (silvopasture is polyculture-by-construction; "dominant layer" is information loss) materially changing. **Out of scope.** Code changes (none, by design); per-guild breakdown line in the tooltip text (Slice M's space); layer-aware *icons* on the tooltip (canopy/midstory/understory glyphs ÔÇö distinct from color-tint, worth a separate design conversation); changes to the existing `LAYER_TINT` palette on the map's per-member geometries (those remain correct ÔÇö per-member geometries genuinely belong to a single layer); light/dark theming (separate deferral). **Verification.** No code change ÔåÆ no tests to run, no tsc to check, no preview-server to verify. The slice's deliverable is this log entry + the ADR; both are reviewable in `git log`. **Invariants preserved.** Every B4 invariant from earlier ADRs holds verbatim ÔÇö no surface has been touched. Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N shipped as code; **O shipped as a documented rejection**. Remaining: **Slice L** (multi-pin ÔÇö substantial slice; needs design conversation about whether the "steward wants to compare 2+ hosts side-by-side" use case is real before committing) and **Slice M** (hover-card drill-down ÔÇö depends on L's per-block addressability).
- [2026-05-30 ÔÇö B4 tooltip i18n seam (Slice N)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-i18n-seam.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice N of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap by shipping the small-path option (path 2): extracts every English string the tooltip surfaces into a new colocated `tooltipStrings.ts` module with a clean seam for future i18next adoption, **without** bootstrapping i18next project-wide. **What changed.** New `apps/web/src/v3/plan/layers/tooltipStrings.ts`: `tooltipStrings` const object holds 3 row labels (`unionFootprint` = "Union footprint", `rawDiskSum` = "Raw ¤Ç┬Àr┬▓ sum", `savedOverlap` = "Saved overlap"); two formatter functions encapsulate the unit-suffix + pluralization logic ÔÇö `formatAreaM2(n)` rounds + appends " m┬▓", `formatHostCounts(guildCount, memberCount)` renders the counts line with English n===1 binary pluralization ("guild"/"guilds", "member"/"members"), the " ┬À " separator, and the "canopy-bearing" qualifier all baked in. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` removes its inline `formatM2` helper, imports the three exports, swaps inline ternaries for the formatter call, and replaces bare string literals with `{tooltipStrings.unionFootprint}` etc. 6 formatter unit tests pin area rounding (incl. 0.49 ÔåÆ "0 m┬▓" toward-zero edge) + plural/singular/zero-as-plural combinations. **Why path 2 not path 1.** `react-i18next` + `i18next` are deps but **zero** `useTranslation` / `i18n.init` call sites exist anywhere in `apps/web/src` ÔÇö the tooltip would be the first consumer. Path 1 would force five ADR-worthy decisions in this slice's scope: bootstrap location, `<I18nextProvider>` wrapper near the app root (startup-time + pending Atlas-portal SSR consideration), resource-file layout (namespace boundaries), bundle-size assessment (~30kB gzipped naively bundled), and a project-wide copy-migration policy. The constants module gets the strings *organised* without forcing any of those bets; path 1 stays available as a follow-up when a second locale is confirmed. **Why a TS module, not a JSON resource file.** JSON is standard i18next layout but can't hold the formatter functions ÔÇö splitting them now would leave a half-organised seam. When i18next lands, formatters become a thin shim around `t()` and the string-constant object migrates to JSON; the file shrinks or disappears. **Why keep English n===1 in-module.** A real i18n library will replace it with CLDR plural rules per locale (Arabic: six forms; Russian: three). Current formatter signature `(count, count) => string` is narrow on purpose ÔÇö future swap to `t('tooltip.hostCounts', { guildCount, memberCount })` requires no call-site changes. **Migration recipe documented** in the module header docstring: (1) add `apps/web/src/i18n/index.ts` i18next bootstrap, (2) wrap `<App />` in `<I18nextProvider>`, (3) swap `tooltipStrings.foo` for `t('tooltip.foo')`, (4) move values into `locales/en/tooltip.json`, (5) delete the module. **Strings preserved byte-identically.** Row labels, " m┬▓" suffix, " ┬À " separator, "canopy-bearing" qualifier, n===1 binary pluralization ÔÇö all unchanged. The existing tooltip rendering tests pass without modification, strong evidence the refactor changed nothing observable. **Verification.** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers` ÔåÆ 24/24 (12 tooltip + 6 memberDragMath + 6 new tooltipStrings); `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` ÔåÆ 284/284 (36 files; +6 over Slice K); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files; preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success" ÔÇö refactor is a pure extraction whose visible output is byte-identical per the unchanged rendering tests. **Invariants preserved.** All Slice K (scroll-cap carve-out, data-scrollable threshold=4), J / I / H, and earlier B4 invariants (mouseleave-driven dismiss in hover mode + small-pinned, single-pin, multi-feature fan-out, touch tap-outside dismiss, enter + exit + per-block + reverse-in-flight fade, `prefers-reduced-motion`). **Out of scope.** Bootstrapping i18next (path 1, deferred); extracting strings from any other surface (tooltip-only by scope); number formatting beyond m┬▓ (decimal separators, grouping ÔÇö available once i18next lands); RTL layout (separate infrastructure decision ÔÇö CSS logical properties + `[dir]` attribute on `<html>`). Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N shipped; next is **Slice O** (per-layer tinted accent stripe ÔÇö research/decision step first, may ship as a "still rejected" ADR rather than code) per the approved execution order.
- [2026-05-30 ÔÇö B4 tooltip max-height scroll cap (Slice K)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-scroll-cap.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice K of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap ÔÇö the highest-risk wave-C entry because **any** scroll affordance on the host-canopy-union tooltip requires `pointer-events: auto`, which collides with the 2026-05-25 invariant that the tooltip must NEVER steal the underlying union layer's mouseleave. **The carve-out.** `.tooltip[data-scrollable='true']` activates only when `pinned=true AND entries.length >= 4`. The CSS rule adds `max-height: calc(100vh - 80px)`, `overflow-y: auto`, and `pointer-events: auto`. Below either condition the invariant survives verbatim: hover mode + any host count = `pointer-events: none` and mouseleave-driven dismiss; pinned + 1ÔÇô3 hosts = same. Above both conditions, mouseleave is moot ÔÇö when pinned, dismissal is via ESC, click-again-on-host, or tap-outside-canvas-and-outside-tooltip, none of which depend on the tooltip's pointer-events. **Tap-outside handler carve-out (PlanDataLayers).** `onDocPointerDown` would have dismissed pointerdowns on the tooltip's scrollbar/content (target not in canvas ÔåÆ fall through). New early-return: `if (target instanceof Element && target.closest('[data-testid="host-canopy-union-tooltip"]')) return;`. The tooltip is portalled to the document body so PlanDataLayers can't hold a ref to it ÔÇö the data-testid already used by tests becomes the production query selector, no portal-aware ref forwarding needed. **Edge-clamp adjustment.** Raw `entries.length * PER_BLOCK_H` would over-reserve vertical space when the surface is scroll-capped (e.g. 20-host pinned stack) and push the anchor unnecessarily high; new `scrollCapMaxH = Math.max(PER_BLOCK_H, viewportH - 80)` bounds the estimatedH when `scrollable`. `Math.max(PER_BLOCK_H, ...)` guards against pathologically short viewports. **Threshold = 4.** Three hosts (~340px) fits 768px viewport comfortably; four (~448px) tight; five+ clips. Single `SCROLL_CAP_THRESHOLD = 4` module constant so a future tuning round can move it without touching consumers. **Reserve = 80px.** `calc(100vh - 80px)` matches the existing edge-clamp's intuitive budget (12px cursor gap + 8px padding at top/bottom + DesignToolRail headroom); on a 720px viewport ~640px usable Ôëê 5.9 blocks, "scroll if you must" not "scroll constantly." **Why not WAAPI / wheel-capture.** The roadmap's alternative ÔÇö capture `wheel` events on the document, translate to a CSS-variable offset on a virtual scrollable container ÔÇö would preserve the 2026-05-25 invariant verbatim but re-implement overscroll, inertia, scrollbar-drag, keyboard scroll, and require a separate `touchmove` path for tablets. The dual carve-out (CSS + tap-outside) ships in ~10 lines and inherits every native scroll affordance for free; the narrow carve-out window keeps the invariant holding in every state the steward meets during normal hover flow. **Why threshold-by-entry-count not viewport-bound.** The cleaner predicate would be `scrollable = pinned && rawEstimatedH > scrollCapMaxH`, but (a) entries.length is stable across viewport changes (resize doesn't toggle the carve-out under a pinned steward) and (b) the test surface stays simpler. If the fixed threshold proves wrong for small viewports, swap the predicate without changing the data-attribute contract. **Reused, not built:** existing portal mount; existing data-testid; existing tap-outside listener; existing edge-clamp logic; existing fade machinery (data-visible / data-exiting / transition tokens). **Tests added:** 4 under `scroll-cap carve-out (Slice K)` describe ÔÇö below-threshold pinned = no data-scrollable; above-threshold unpinned = no data-scrollable (hover invariant survives); at-threshold pinned = data-scrollable='true'; very-tall (20-host) pinned at viewport-top = data-scrollable='true' + edge-clamp produces non-negative top (regression guard). **Verification:** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers/__tests__/HostCanopyUnionTooltip.test.tsx` ÔåÆ 12/12 (8 prior + 4 new); `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` ÔåÆ 278/278 (35 files; +4 over Slice J); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on the three touched files (pre-existing unrelated errors elsewhere unchanged); preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success" ÔÇö data-attribute contract fully unit-test-covered, visible scroll relies on browser-native `overflow-y: auto`. **Invariants preserved:** 2026-05-25 (mouseleave-driven dismiss in hover mode + pinned-small-stack), 2026-05-26 (single-pin), 2026-05-27 (multi-feature fan-out), 2026-05-28 (touch tap-outside dismiss), 2026-05-29 + 30 (enter + exit + per-block + reverse-in-flight fade), `prefers-reduced-motion`. **Out of scope:** Slice L multi-pin (separate slice; depends on this one), Slice M hover-card drill-down (depends on L), viewport-aware predicate, sticky block headers when scrolling, keyboard arrow-key navigation between blocks. Roadmap status: H + I + J + K shipped; next is **Slice N** (tooltip i18n small path) per the approved execution order.
- [2026-05-30 ÔÇö B4 InlineFeaturePopover exit fade (Slice J)](log/2026-05-30-b4-inline-popover-exit-fade.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice J of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap, consuming the `--motion-overlay-*` tokens added in Slice I. Click-driven inline mini-form `InlineFeaturePopover` adopts the same deferred-unmount machinery the 2026-05-30 host-canopy-union tooltip ship landed: a `displayed: InlineFormPayload | null` mirror state lives one exit-transition longer than `useInlineFormStore.active`, `exiting: boolean` flips at the same time `active` goes null, `visible: boolean` flips via `useLayoutEffect` after mount so the enter transition fires from `opacity: 0`/`translateY(2px)` ÔåÆ `opacity: 1`/`translateY(0)`. CSS-Module `.popover` rule gains the from-state + `transition: opacity var(--motion-overlay-duration) var(--motion-overlay-ease-out), transform var(--motion-overlay-duration) var(--motion-overlay-ease-out)`. New `.popover[data-visible='true']` selector targets the visible state; new `.popover[data-exiting='true']` mirrors the from-state, switches the easing token to `--motion-overlay-ease-in`, and adds **`pointer-events: none`** so a mid-fade click on a fading Save/Cancel button is physically impossible. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` block nulls both transitions so reduced-motion users see instant dismissal. **The interactivity invariant difference from the tooltip.** Tooltip is `pointer-events: none` ÔÇö invariant: "must never steal events from the underlying layer." Popover is `pointer-events: auto` ÔÇö owns inputs, Save, Cancel, custom actions. So the tooltip's invariant doesn't transfer. New invariant: **a mid-fade click on a fading button must not race the displayed-mirror cleanup.** Defense-in-depth: exit-state CSS drops `pointer-events: none` (primary defence), Save/Cancel handlers also guard on `if (!active)` (free insurance ÔÇö store entry has cleared by the time exit starts). **Value-reset block now skips active=null.** Pre-fade logic unconditionally cleared `values` when `active` went null; with deferred unmount the form renders through the fade and clearing values mid-fade would visually empty every input. New logic only resets when active becomes a **new non-null payload**; active going null is the exit signal and values stay frozen until `displayed` clears. **`onPopoverTransitionEnd` filters on three conditions.** `propertyName === 'opacity'` (rejects the transform-property transitionend so the unmount is deterministic and tied to the visually-disappearing property), `target === currentTarget` (rejects bubbled child transitionends from nested `<input>`, `<select>`, `<button>` focus-ring + hover-state transitions), `exiting === true` (rejects post-reverse-in-flight transitionends that would spuriously unmount a restored form). 200ms safety `setTimeout` covers `prefers-reduced-motion` where transitionend never fires. **Render guard switched from `if (!active) return null` ÔåÆ `if (!displayed) return null`** so the form stays mounted through the fade; title, fields, customActions iteration all read from `displayed`. New 4-test suite `InlineFeaturePopover.test.tsx` pins: cold-start renders nothing; `open()` mounts with `data-visible='true'`; `close()` flips `data-exiting='true'`, transform-property transitionend does NOT unmount but opacity-property transitionend does; reverse-in-flight `open()` during exit restores form and subsequent opacity transitionend does not spuriously unmount. Uses the same `fireTransitionEnd(el, propertyName)` `Object.defineProperty` happy-dom helper as the 2026-05-30 tooltip tests. **Reused, not built:** Slice I `--motion-overlay-*` tokens; deferred-unmount pattern from the 2026-05-30 tooltip ship; existing ESC + click-outside listeners (still gated on `active` so they auto-detach at exit start ÔÇö correct, because the form is no longer interactive). **Invariants preserved:** schema-driven render (title, fields, customActions, required-field gate, disclosure expansion) unchanged; ESC + click-outside dismiss; reduced-motion behaviour. **Out of scope:** the slide-up dialog used for written reports (different surface class ÔÇö slide-up animation, not fade); cubic-bezier alignment of overlay surfaces with the project's `--ease-out`/`--ease-in` family (deferred per the Slice I ADR; revisit when a third consumer arrives); per-field exit animations within the popover. **Verification:** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` ÔåÆ 274/274 green (35 files; +4 new InlineFeaturePopover tests; 8/8 tooltip tests untouched); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files (pre-existing unrelated errors in `LandAssessmentSlideUp.tsx`, `AtlasAIPanel.tsx`, `HydrologyRightPanel.tsx` confirmed unchanged via baseline grep); preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree (Vite resolves against worktree-root `node_modules` which doesn't exist) ÔÇö stated explicitly per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success," structurally identical to the 2026-05-30 tooltip ship whose contract is fully unit-test-covered. Roadmap status: H + I + J shipped; next is **Slice K** (max-height scroll cap when N hosts is large) which carries the `pointer-events` carve-out risk.
- [2026-05-30 ÔÇö B4 motion-token harmonisation (Slice I)](log/2026-05-30-b4-motion-token-harmonisation.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice I of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap. Extracts the four hard-coded overlay-fade literals from `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.module.css` (duration `120ms`, translate `2px`, easing `ease-out`/`ease-in`) into a new `--motion-overlay-*` token family declared on `:root` in [apps/web/src/styles/tokens.css](../apps/web/src/styles/tokens.css) alongside the existing `--duration-*` / `--ease-*` families. Four sites of `transition: opacity 120ms ease-... , transform 120ms ease-...` rewritten as `var(...)` calls; three `translateY(2px)` sites likewise. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` block unchanged (nulls `transition` entirely, no per-token override needed). **Why a new family, not reuse `--duration-*` / `--ease-*`.** Existing duration ladder is 100/200/400/600ms; tooltip's 120ms was tuned because 100ms felt snappy and 200ms felt draggy under cursor motion. Existing `--ease-out`/`--ease-in` are cubic-beziers (`cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)` / `cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)`); tooltip ships with bare CSS keywords (`cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.58, 1)` / `cubic-bezier(0.42, 0, 1, 1)`). Coercing to either would ship a visual change as part of a "token extraction" slice. New family preserves literals verbatim; cubic-bezier alignment deferred to a follow-up ADR after Slice J's adoption verifies the current curves feel right with two consumers. **Why CSS custom properties, not TS constants.** CSS Modules can't reference TS without inline `style={{}}` (loses scoping) or a CSS-in-JS pipeline (overkill for four literals). The 200ms safety timeout in `PlanDataLayers.tsx` does duplicate `--motion-overlay-duration + slack`, but the slack is the load-bearing part ÔÇö if a second JS consumer materialises we'll revisit. **Why these four tokens specifically.** Two easings (not one) because enter accelerates toward the visible state and exit decelerates away from it; CSS variables can't carry direction. One duration (not three) because the 2026-05-30 ship uses 120ms across enter / exit / reverse-in-flight ÔÇö different durations per intent would be a design change, not extraction. **Tokens.css is already imported once at the app root via [app/index.css:6](../apps/web/src/app/index.css), so no additional wiring needed and CSS custom properties propagate through the cascade into CSS-Modules-scoped class names.** Tests untouched ÔÇö contract tests only assert data-attrs + event handling, neither affected by value extraction. 8/8 tooltip + 63/63 agroforestry green. Touched files TS-clean. **Unlocks Slice J** (InlineFeaturePopover exit fade) which can adopt the same tokens at birth so the two map-overlay surfaces fade in sync. Roadmap deferrals: cubic-bezier alignment, dark-mode-only overrides, additional surface-class families (`--motion-modal-*` etc) all kept deferred.

- [2026-05-30 ÔÇö B4 follow-up: per-block tooltip fade + reverse-in-flight](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-perblock-fade-and-reverse.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the last two still-deferred bullets from the 2026-05-29 exit-fade ADR: per-block exit fade in multi-host stacks, and reverse-in-flight animation when `activeUnion` returns non-null mid-exit. Fade machinery refactored from CSS keyframes (`@keyframes tooltipFadeIn` / `tooltipFadeOut`) to **CSS transitions** on opacity + transform; `.tooltip` mounts at `opacity: 0` and `.tooltip[data-visible='true']` flips to `opacity: 1` (the enter transition fires from a `useLayoutEffect` that sets `visible=true` on mount); `.tooltip[data-exiting='true']` takes opacity back to 0 with `ease-in` timing. New `.hostBlock` rule mirrors the same shape for per-block fades. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` override nulls all four selectors' `transition`. **Reverse-in-flight is free** with transitions: removing `data-exiting` mid-fade lets the transition interpolate from the current visible value back to 1, with no snap and no JS ÔÇö making the 2026-05-29 monotonic-key remount pattern unnecessary. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` exports a new `HostBlockEntry` interface (hostId + per-entry `phase: 'entering' | 'exiting'`); `HostBlock` renders `data-testid='host-block-${hostId}'`, `data-exiting='true'` when phase==='exiting', and an `onTransitionEnd` filtered by `propertyName==='opacity'` + `target===currentTarget` that fires a new `onEntryExited?: (hostId: string) => void` prop. Container's own `onTransitionEnd` filters by both `propertyName==='opacity'` and `target===currentTarget` so bubbled per-block transitionends don't fire `onExited`. **Merge-by-hostId.** `PlanDataLayers.displayedUnion` state shape replaces 2026-05-29's `key + entries: HostBlock[]` with per-entry phase tracking (`entries: HostBlockEntry[]`); the monotonic key is gone. The mirror `useEffect` rewrites the merge: kept hosts (in both old and new sets) carry forward with phase `entering` and refreshed data; dropped hosts (in old but not new) flip to phase `exiting` and stay in the array; new hosts are appended in MapLibre topmost-first order. The React `key` on the rendered map iterator is now `entry.hostId` (stable per host) so a block's in-flight transition isn't cancelled when siblings drop out and the array re-indexes. `onEntryExited` callback drops the hostId from the entries array ÔÇö or clears the mirror entirely if the last block just finished fading. Safety timeout bumped 180 ÔåÆ 200 ms (120 ms transition + 80 ms slack to absorb event-loop jitter and the `prefers-reduced-motion` instant-change case where transitionend doesn't fire). **Test scaffolding.** New `fireTransitionEnd(el, propertyName)` helper ÔÇö `@testing-library/dom`'s `createEvent.transitionEnd` passes init to the constructor without a fallback, and happy-dom's `TransitionEvent` constructor silently drops the `propertyName` init key, so the helper `Object.defineProperty`'s the value onto the event post-construction. Existing tests migrated from `fireEvent.animationEnd({ animationName: 'tooltipFadeOut' })` to the new helper. Two new tests: reverse-in-flight asserts that flipping `exiting` from true ÔåÆ false during re-render clears `data-exiting` and a subsequent opacity transitionend does NOT fire `onExited`; per-block exit asserts that an entry with `phase='exiting'` carries `data-exiting='true'`, that opacity transitionend fires `onEntryExited(hostId)`, and that sibling `entering` blocks + transform-property transitionends do not. **Why transitions, not WAAPI.** The 2026-05-29 ADR speculated about `element.animate()` + `animation.reverse()`. Transitions get the same behaviour with zero JS: they always interpolate from the current computed value, which is exactly what "reverse" means for a single-property fade. **Why merge by hostId.** When the active set shrinks, the dropped host has to stay in the displayed array long enough to fade; indices shift under set changes, so a key-by-index would cancel its transition when the array re-reconciled. Invariants preserved: `pointer-events: none`, single-pin model, ESC + tap-outside-to-dismiss, multi-feature fan-out (2026-05-27), edge-clamp + entries-aware `ESTIMATED_H` (counts every block including phase-`exiting` ones so a tooltip about to lose a block stays clamped conservatively ÔÇö no flicker-reposition mid-fade), reduced-motion behaviour (was: no keyframe animation; now: no transition). 71/71 vitest green (8 tooltip + 63 agroforestry; +2 tooltip tests over the 2026-05-29 ship). Touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-29 ADR reverse-in-flight + per-block bullets flipped open ÔåÆ closed.

- [2026-05-21 ÔÇö fix(web): Vite dev proxy translates ECONNREFUSED into API_OFFLINE envelope](log/2026-05-21-vite-proxy-api-offline-envelope.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the "Response not JSON (500)" papercut on `POST /api/v1/auth/register` from `http://localhost:5200/login`. Confirmed via `Test-NetConnection` + direct `/health` probe that nothing was listening on port 3001; the 500 was Vite's dev proxy returning plain-text HTML for `ECONNREFUSED`, not the API (whose global `setErrorHandler` in `apps/api/src/app.ts` *always* sends a JSON envelope, so a non-JSON 500 cannot originate there). Added `configure` + `proxy.on('error', ÔÇª)` to the `/api` entry in `apps/web/vite.config.ts` that emits a `503` carrying the API's own envelope shape `{ data: null, error: { code: 'API_OFFLINE', message: "API server unreachable at http://localhost:3001 (<errno>). Start it with:  pnpm --filter @ogden/api dev" } }`. `apiClient.ts` flows the envelope through unchanged ÔåÆ LoginPage `role="alert"` banner renders the actionable instruction verbatim. Iterated once on the message format ÔÇö first draft wrapped the command in backticks; when an operator pasted the banner verbatim into PowerShell, the backticks parsed as line-continuation and `(ECONNREFUSED)` as a sub-expression call. Plain-text form is copy-paste safe. Verified in live preview: API stopped ÔåÆ in-page `fetch('/api/v1/auth/register')` returned `503` + envelope, LoginPage banner DOM matched verbatim, console error stream flipped from `ApiError: Response not JSON (500)` to `ApiError: API server unreachable ÔÇª` at the moment Vite picked up the config change; API restarted ÔåÆ same call returned `201` + `{ token, user }`. No edits to auth routes (`apps/api/src/routes/auth/index.ts` was sound), no new migrations, no dev seed-user script (explicitly declined ÔÇö permanent fix only). - [2026-05-29 ÔÇö B4 follow-up: tooltip exit fade](log/2026-05-29-b4-tooltip-exit-fade.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the last fade-related still-deferred bullet from the 2026-05-25 host-union-hover-tooltip ADR (deferred again on 2026-05-28): animated fade **out**. `PlanDataLayers.tsx` gets a third `useState` (`displayedUnion`) that mirrors `activeUnion = pinnedUnion ?? hoveredUnion` but lives one exit-animation longer, with `phase: 'entering' | 'exiting'` and a monotonic `key`. A `useEffect([activeUnion])` writes the mirror synchronously on non-null `activeUnion` (fresh `key` remounts the tooltip so the enter keyframe replays ÔÇö covers re-enter during in-flight exit) and flips the mirror's phase to `'exiting'` on null `activeUnion`. A 180 ms safety `setTimeout` (120 ms anim + 60 ms slack) covers the `prefers-reduced-motion` short-circuit case where `animationend` never fires. Portal-render now reads `displayedUnion`, forwards `key`, `exiting`, and `onExited`, and forces `pinned={false}` during exit so the gold accent doesn't linger. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` props extended with optional `exiting?` + `onExited?`; root `<div>` gets conditional `data-exiting='true'` and an `onAnimationEnd` handler that fires `onExited()` when `exiting === true` and `animationName.includes('tooltipFadeOut')` (CSS Modules scopes the keyframe name; `.includes` matches the scoped form). `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.module.css` adds `@keyframes tooltipFadeOut` (opacity 1ÔåÆ0, translateY 0ÔåÆ2px ÔÇö the reverse of the enter keyframe); `.tooltip[data-exiting='true'] { animation: tooltipFadeOut 120ms ease-in forwards; }` ÔÇö `forwards` holds the final state until React unmount. The `prefers-reduced-motion` media block extended to null both keyframes. New test asserts `data-exiting` forwarding + `onExited` fires on `tooltipFadeOut` animationend and NOT on unrelated keyframe names. Why not `useRef` or `useReducer`: refs don't trigger re-render (the portal-branch needs to subscribe); two-shape state machine doesn't justify reducer boilerplate. Why force `pinned=false` during exit: gold accent reads "sticky," fade reads "going away" ÔÇö stacking confuses the surface. Invariants preserved: `pointer-events: none`, single-pin, single-tooltip, multi-feature fan-out, edge-clamp, enter fade, tap-outside dismiss. 69/69 vitest green (6 tooltip + 63 agroforestry). Touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-25 + 2026-05-28 ADR exit-fade bullets flipped to closed.

New `apps/api/src/services/ai/agentRegistry.ts` exports `AgentRole` (`'agro-designer' | 'hydro-engineer' | 'general'`), a static role-prompt table, pure `routeIntent(text): AgentRole` (case-insensitive word-boundary keyword tally ÔÇö hydro: `swale`, `keyline`, `pond`, `water`, `hydro`, `runoff`, `infiltration`, `drainage`, `riparian`, `aquifer`, `cistern`, `dam`, `creek`, `flood`; agro: `orchard`, `paddock`, `tree`, `plant`, `species`, `crop`, `pasture`, `grazing`, `livestock`, `rotation`, `cover crop`, `compost`, `silvopasture`; ties or zero ÔåÆ `'general'`), `resolveRole`, and `runAgent(input)` which composes the role addendum, calls `chatWithRole`, and parses any trailing `HANDOFF: <role> ÔÇö <reason>` line (en-dash `ÔÇö` or ASCII `--` separator) into `handoff: { to, reason } | null` (server does not auto-chain ÔÇö caller decides). New route `POST /api/v1/ai/agent-chat` appended to `apps/api/src/routes/ai/index.ts` with `authenticate + resolveProjectRole` preHandlers (project-membership gate). 24-case test suite `apps/api/src/tests/aiAgents.test.ts` mirrors the `ClaudeClient.test.ts` global-`fetch`-stub pattern: `routeIntent` purity, `parseHandoff` positives + negatives + ASCII separator + malformed role, `resolveRole` precedence, `runAgent` end-to-end (composes the 2-block system array with the cached base prompt verbatim, autoRoutes, defaults to general, parses handoff, forwards usage tokens) and a direct `chatWithRole` unit test. **C.7 (`6a61d6cf`)** lands `apps/web/src/features/livestock/engine/rotationEngine.ts` (`computeRotationCalendar({ paddocks, herdSize, animalUnitMonths?, parasiteBreakDays = 60, grazeDaysPerPaddock = 3 }): RotationCalendar`) ÔÇö wraps canonical `computeRotationCarryingCapacity` via a synthetic single-mob `RotationPlan` (every paddock in one cell group, `targetGrazeDays = grazeDaysPerPaddock`, `targetRestDays = parasiteBreakDays`) plus mob-grazed paddock list with per-paddock `stockingDensity = herdSize / areaHa` so the AU math is never forked; `cycleDays = grazeDaysPerPaddock ├ù paddocks.length`; `recoveryDays = cycleDays ÔêÆ grazeDaysPerPaddock`; `annualAuDays = herdSize ├ù 365`; `cyclesPerYear = floor(365 / cycleDays)`; `parasiteBreakCompliant = every entry's recoveryDays ÔëÑ parasiteBreakDays`; degenerate input (no paddocks or `grazeDaysPerPaddock Ôëñ 0`) returns a well-formed zero calendar (`entries: []`, `cycleDays: 0`, `cyclesPerYear: 0`, vacuously compliant, `status: 'ok'`). New `apps/web/src/features/financial/engine/livestockRevenue.ts` (`buildLivestockRevenueStream(calendar, { pricePerAuDay, startYear = 1, maturityYear?, confidence = 'medium', assumptions?, id?, name? })`) ÔÇö `annualRevenue.{low,mid,high} = pricePerAuDay.{...} ├ù annualAuDays` (rounded); default 5-year build-up ramp `[0.2, 0.4, 0.65, 0.85, 1.0]` plateauing at 1.0 through year 10; `startYear` shifts the ramp; `assumptions[]` surfaces herd ├ù 365 AU-days, rotation cycle + paddock count, parasite-break compliance line (Ô£ô "Parasite-break floor met (Xd minimum rest)" vs Ô£ù "WARNING: parasite-break floor NOT met ÔÇö recovery Yd < Xd"), utilization + status, plus caller-supplied lines; default `enterprise: 'livestock'`. The stream slots into `computeCashflow([], [stream], phases, horizon)` with **zero engine change**. `RotationScheduleCard.tsx` gains an additive "Cycle engine" summary block between the status pills row and the per-group timelines: `cyclesPerYear`, `annualAuDays` (locale-formatted), parasite-break compliance badge (green ÔëÑ 60d / amber < 60d), and utilization % with status pill (`ok` / `tight` / `over`). Card doesn't track herd size today, so the block uses an implied-mob heuristic of ~1 AU/ha (`Math.max(1, round(totalHa))`) ÔÇö clearly labelled in the header hint so stewards know it's a placeholder until herd-size capture lands. Existing ad-hoc moves table below is untouched per [[feedback_no_deletion]]; plan-driven `RotationSequenceCard.tsx` is left alone. 16 new tests (8 rotation-engine + 8 livestock-revenue) cover: 11 ├ù 3-day graze ÔåÆ `cycleDays 33`, `recoveryDays 30`, parasite-break NOT met; 11 ├ù 6-day graze ÔåÆ `cycleDays 66`, `recoveryDays 60`, compliant; 50 AU ├ù 365 = 18,250 AU-days; 200-acre fixture at 1 AU / 2 acres ÔåÆ 36,500 AU-days; contiguous startDay sequence; degenerate empty + zero-herd paths; utilization roll-up; `annualRevenue.mid = pricePerAuDay.mid ├ù annualAuDays`; enterprise tag; ramp 0 before startYear + monotone non-decreasing through plateau; startYear shift; WARNING / Parasite-break-floor-met assumptions; end-to-end `computeCashflow` integration (year-0 = 0, year-1 > 0, year-10 ÔëÑ year-1). Gate: API tsc clean; `pnpm --filter @ogden/api run test` **653 passed / 3 skipped (656)** across 60 files; web tsc shows only pre-existing `StepBoundary.tsx(365,7)` `unknownÔåÆReactNode` foreign-WIP error (verified via stash-baseline comparison); `pnpm --filter @ogden/web run test` **1620 passed (1620)** across 157 files (incl. 24 C.6 + 16 C.7 new cases). Manual 200-acre fixture smoke deferred per Assumption A2. Covenant + IA preserved: no CSRA / *bay╩┐ m─ü laysa ╩┐indak* / salam framing reintroduced; "capital partners & allies" language preserved (livestock revenue is steward-facing operating estimate, not investor yield); 3-item Observe/Plan/Act IA unchanged; mobile Overview stack stays flat (engine block lands on the card, not the mobile shell). - [2026-05-27 ÔÇö B4 follow-up: multi-feature fan-out on host-union tooltip](log/2026-05-27-b4-union-tooltip-multi-feature-fanout.md) ÔÇö **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the "Multi-feature fan-out when `resolveSilvopastureHosts` ever produces overlapping hosts" still-deferred bullet on the 2026-05-25 host-union-hover-tooltip ADR. The 2026-05-25 + 2026-05-26 ships both read only `e.features?.[0]` ÔÇö when two silvopasture polygons spatially overlap (silvopastureHosts enumerator unions cropAreas + designElements with no dedup), the steward sees only one host's three m┬▓ values. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip` props refactored: new exported `HostBlockProps` interface; top-level shape becomes `{ point, entries: HostBlockProps[], pinned? }` (flat single-host fields removed, no backward-compat shim). Render loops `entries.map((e, i) => ...)` with `<hr className={styles.separator} role="separator" />` between consecutive blocks (single-host stacks omit the separator entirely ÔÇö visually identical to the 2026-05-26 ship). `HostBlock` sub-component lifted local to the file. Edge-clamp `ESTIMATED_H` now `entries.length`-aware (`BASE_H + entries.length * PER_BLOCK_H` ~ 16 + 108┬Àn) so the bottom-edge anchor flip keeps a 3-block tooltip on-screen at the gutter. CSS adds `.separator` hairline rule (`#f2ede3` family at 0.12 opacity against the dark glass). `PlanDataLayers` state widened: `hoveredUnion` / `pinnedUnion` carry `entries: HostBlock[]` (`HostBlock = HostBlockProps & { hostId: string }`); pinned additionally keeps a sorted `hostIds: string[]` for set-equality unpin. `unpackProps` ÔåÆ `unpackEntries` walks every entry in `e.features` (not `[0]`), filters by `properties.kind === 'host-canopy-union'`, dedups by `hostId` via `Set` (MapLibre can emit the same Feature twice when its source has multiple visible tiles intersecting the cursor). Click toggle now uses `sameHostIdSet` sorted-array equality: clicking a stack whose `hostIds` set matches the pinned stack's unpins; any other click replaces. Hover-suppression-while-pinned and ESC unpin unchanged. Portal render forwards `entries` instead of spread props. Why vertical stack, not tabs / chooser: any in-tooltip interactivity (tabs, hover-card-to-expand, chooser) would force `pointer-events: auto` and break the 2026-05-25 non-negotiable that the tooltip never steals `mouseleave` from the underlying union-fill. Stacking is the only design that holds the invariant. 1 new render test (two-host stack: both names visible, both sets of m┬▓ values rendered, exactly one `role="separator"` between); 4 existing tests migrated to length-1 `entries`. 5/5 tooltip + 63/63 agroforestry green; touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-25 ADR's multi-feature-fan-out bullet flipped open ÔåÆ closed.

## 2026-05-31 - Wizard light-mode theming + bento section cards

**Commit:** 020dd913 (feat/atlas-permaculture, pushed 0/0)

**Objective:** Make the project-creation wizard honor the app light/dark toggle
(it was stuck dark) and replace horizontal divider lines with bordered bento
cards across every section of every step.

**Root cause (light-mode bug):** every project-wizard/*.module.css referenced an
undefined legacy token namespace (--surface-*, --text-*, --border-*, --accent-*)
with hardcoded dark hex fallbacks, plus bare dark literals (rgba(14,20,19,a)
glass, #0e1413 button text, gold/amber tints, rgba(232,225,208,a) hover). With
the tokens undefined, CSS always fell back to the dark hex, so the wizard never
flipped.

**Change 1 - token migration (17 CSS modules):** mapped all legacy/hardcoded
values onto canonical --color-* tokens that flip per data-theme: surfaces ->
--color-bg / --color-surface / --color-surface-raised; borders ->
--color-border(-subtle); text -> --color-text(-muted); accents ->
--color-gold-brand / --color-primary-hover / --color-warning / --color-success
/ --color-error; map glass -> rgba(var(--color-map-panel-rgb), a); gold/amber
tints -> rgba(var(--color-*-rgb), a); button text on gold -> --color-on-primary;
hover -> --color-hover-overlay. One inline style in WizardStepRouter.tsx fixed
too. tokens.css / dark-mode.css left untouched (out of scope).

**Change 2 - bento cards:** added a shared .bento card (border 1px
--color-border-subtle, radius 12px, bg --color-surface, padding 16px) to Steps
1-3; wrapped each section in its own card (Step 1: name / country+address /
units; Step 2: project-type grid / secondary layers; Step 3: primary steward);
dropped the unused Step 2 .divider rule; converted the Step 3 invites group from
a border-top divider into a full card. WizardTensionPanel and the Completion
.nextUp were already cards, left as-is.

**Verification:** typecheck clean (TSC_EXIT=0); grep LEGACY=0 across all wizard
CSS; CSS_BENTO=3, TSX_BENTO_USES=6, Step2 divider=0, Step3 border-top=0. Guarded
staging committed ONLY the 21 project-wizard files (foreign WIP -
Diagnose/Design/OperateMap, financial files, graphify-out - correctly excluded).

**Note:** preview light/dark screenshots were NOT captured this session - the
tool-result channel was severely degraded (sustained buffering/outage), so per
project policy this is recorded as unverified-by-screenshot rather than claimed.
Visual confirmation in both themes remains a follow-up.

**Deferred:** light+dark preview screenshots of the wizard steps.

## 2026-05-31 -- Wizard chrome fixes: DecisionRail removal + whole-page scroll

Two issues the operator reported on the live Project Creation Wizard, fixed on
`feat/atlas-permaculture`, commit `76499f4e` (2 files, +20/-6), NOT pushed
(operator chose commit-only: branch was 6 ahead / 0 behind origin, with 5 foreign
WIP commits below mine that must not be published).

- **Fix 1 - DecisionRail leaked onto wizard steps 2/3.** `apps/web/src/v3/V3ProjectLayout.tsx` -
  `activeFromPath` resolves `/wizard/*` to the "home" stage (not in
  `SELF_RAILED_STAGES`), so the generic DecisionRail rendered on every wizard step.
  Added an `isWizard` path check that forces `rail = undefined` on wizard routes; the
  global header + ProjectBundleBar still render.
- **Fix 2 - whole page scrolled instead of the form section.** `apps/web/src/v3/project-wizard/ProjectWizardShell.module.css` -
  `.shell` measured `height: calc(100vh - header)` but mounts below BOTH the app
  header AND the ProjectBundleBar inside an already-bounded `.outletHost`; the
  bundle-bar overshoot forced a page scroll. Changed to `height: 100%; min-height: 0`
  so it fills the bounded slot. The form column keeps its own `overflow-y: auto;
  min-height: 0`, so tall step content scrolls inside the column.

**Verified (live DOM via preview eval, localhost:5200):**
- DecisionRail removal CONFIRMED - `railPresent: false` on both `/wizard/vision` and
  `/wizard/team`; one run rendered real step-2 content (regions: Workspace content,
  Vision & Capacity, Project type selector, Secondary layer selector) with no rail
  region present.
- Whole-page scroll CONFIRMED fixed - `pageScrollable: false` on both wizard routes.
- Web typecheck TSC_EXIT=0.

**Honesty note:** the form-column internal-scroll behaviour is guaranteed by CSS
construction (`.form overflow-y:auto + min-height:0` inside the now-bounded
`overflow:hidden` shell) and by the prior-session seed-check measurement
(shell-fits-viewport, page non-scrollable), but a clean live tall-content overflow
measurement (scrollHeight > clientHeight) was NOT captured this session - the
headless eval's deep dynamic-route rehydration via pushState was intermittent
(`shellSectionFound` flickered false on single-nav runs). Recorded as
structurally-sound, not pixel-measured, rather than overclaimed.
